Jinan City Levies House Tax 72

Jinan Correspondence: The house tax in this city was first levied by Zhang Zongchang in the autumn of the 14th year of the Republic (1925). It was levied again in the spring of the 17th year of the Republic (1928). After the provincial government moved to Jinan last year, it was decided at a regular meeting to implement the levy of house tax in this fiscal year, which will be handled by the Jinan Municipal Government and has been included in the budget for the 19th year of the Republic (1930). There are two categories: residential house tax and commercial house tax. Residential house tax refers to ordinary people's housing and is levied at 5% of the rental value. At that time, it was estimated that 10,000 households would pay 75 cents each, generating a monthly revenue of $7,500. 20,000 households would pay 30 cents each, generating a monthly revenue of $6,000. The total annual revenue would be $162,000. Commercial house tax refers to businesses and is levied at 10% of the rental value. It is estimated that 5,000 households would pay an average of $2 per month each, generating a total revenue of $10,000 per month. The total annual revenue would be $120,000. Combining both residential and commercial house taxes, the total annual revenue would be $282,000. Subsequently, the case was shelved due to the entry of the Jin army into Jinan and the relocation of the provincial government to Qingdao. Recently, the provincial government revived the old case and repeatedly urged the municipal government to expedite the matter. Mayor Chen Weixin believed that the municipal government's expenses were strained, and the budget was a concern that could not be ignored. Therefore, he ordered the Finance Bureau to actively prepare. As of now, the procedures for levying the tax and the organization of the preparatory office have been determined as follows: (1) The tax rate for residential house tax will still be 5% of the rental value, to be paid by the landlord. The tax rate for commercial house tax will be 10%, to be shared equally between the tenant and the landlord. Poor tenants with a monthly rent of less than $5 will be exempt from the tax to show compassion. Government and school buildings, if they are government property, will be exempt from the tax. If they are rented, the landlord will still be required to pay the house tax. (2) The method of collection will be that the landlord will be responsible for the residential house tax. However, to prevent landlords from raising rents, the municipal government will first cooperate with the party headquarters to organize an evaluation committee to investigate the current rental prices in the city and establish fair regulations. The Finance Bureau will issue a separate rent certificate to the landlord, who will then pay the tax according to the rental price on the rent certificate and will not be allowed to increase the price arbitrarily. The original rent book will be cancelled, and a fee of 10 cents will be charged for the rent certificate. For those who own and live in their own houses, the landlord will estimate the rental value himself and pay the tax according to the regulations. If the estimated rental value is too low, the Finance Bureau may revise it. (3) The organization of the preparatory office. The detailed rules for the organization of the house tax preparatory office have been approved by the municipal government meeting. It will have one director, three clerks in charge of general affairs, accounting, and document affairs, and twelve investigators. (4) The date of commencement of the levy. The preparatory office is expected to complete the investigation by the end of this year and start levying the tax on January 1 of next year. According to Mayor Chen Weixin, the house tax rate in this city is lighter than in other cities in the country. If $200,000 can be collected each year, the municipal expenses can be covered (22nd).

The Story of Zhang Zongchang's Imminent Return to China 73

The Northeast Pities His Poverty and Requests Exemption from Arrest Warrants and the Return of Confiscated Property

Shenyang Correspondence: The rumor that Zhang Zongchang will be reinstated in the Northeast has been spreading recently. Furthermore, figures formerly associated with Zhang Zongchang, such as Lin Xianzhu, the former governor of Shandong, and Cheng Guorui, the former commander of the Third Army, have been actively engaging in activities in Shenyang, attracting the attention of various parties. Given the extremely significant implications of this matter for the current situation, inquiries were made with various relevant parties, revealing that it is far from the truth. Commander Zhang Xueliang, in light of the national disasters and the many disadvantages suffered by the Northeast over the past decade, deeply loathes evil warlords of Zhang Zongchang's ilk. Moreover, during the Feng army's entry into the customs in the 17th year of the Republic (1928), Zhang Zongchang even turned against them. Given his intentions, the Northeast would absolutely not accommodate him. The reason for telegraphing the central government to revoke his arrest warrant and return the previously confiscated property, such as the real estate in Shilaoniang Hutong and Shizi Hutong in Peiping, as well as in Yushu Hutong and various commercial districts in Shenyang, is that after Zhang Zongchang's defeat in Shandong, he has been eking out a precarious existence in the eastern region for years, spending as much as ten million dollars. With his funds depleted and supplies exhausted, Zhang had long sought to return to China during the Central Plains War but was denied permission by various parties, leaving Zhang in a difficult position. He then sent a representative to Zhang Xueliang to plead for permission to take refuge in the Northeast. Zhang, remembering that Zhang Zongchang had followed Zhang Zuolin for many years, felt some sympathy and generously granted his request, simultaneously making representations to the National Government to revoke the arrest warrant and allowing him to return to China and reside temporarily in the Northeast. It is believed that Zhang Zongchang will soon return from Japan. However, the rumors of reinstating Zhang and giving him a position are not true and are merely the baseless claims of Zhang's former subordinates (20th).

Liaoning Legal Entities Discuss Issuing Prize-Winning Bonds 74

To Relieve Financial Panic and Aid Commerce and Agriculture

Shenyang Correspondence: The Liaoning General Chamber of Commerce, Provincial Education Association, Agricultural Association, and Youth Association, legal entities, believe that the province's finances have been exceptionally tight in recent years. Not only have large and small businesses inside and outside the province been collapsing one after another, but farmers in various regions have also reached the point where their finances cannot be sustained. Although the new grain crop has arrived, the price of grain has fallen sharply due to the stagnation of finances, and merchants and farmers are in extreme difficulty. According to someone from Jinxi County, the number of deaths due to debt in the county has recently reached more than 40 in a single month. The main reason is that those in debt cannot fulfill their obligations, and creditors sue in court. Even if the court rules in accordance with the law, they are still unable to enforce the judgment, so the judgment is tantamount to being ineffective. Therefore, no one in the private sector is filing lawsuits in court regarding debt disputes, and many are resorting to force, resulting in a series of deaths and creating the most tragic social phenomenon. As for the police and school institutions in various counties, the financial difficulties in the western Liaoning counties due to the floods are self-evident. Even in the counties with the best harvests, there is currently extreme panic, resulting in police and school salaries being paid partially or being in arrears for three to four months. If this continues, the situation in the various counties will become even more unbearable. Therefore, at 2:00 PM on the 19th, leading figures from various associations held a joint discussion meeting at the Education Association to discuss relief measures and invited Lu Muting, the Director of the Dongsan Province Official Silver Bank, to join the discussion. As a result of the discussion, it was generally agreed that the aforementioned financial difficulties in various counties were purely due to the insufficient distribution of currency circulating throughout the province. According to a recent survey, the currency currently circulating in the province includes 15 million yuan of hard currency issued by the Bianye, China, Jiaotong, and Official Silver Banks' preparation warehouses, and 20 million yuan of Bianye Bank banknotes valued at 14 million yuan in Feng Dayang (the current Feng banknotes have been destroyed many times, leaving only 70 million, valued at 60 yuan as 1 yuan of hard currency, totaling 14 million yuan in hard currency). The Official Silver Bank's newly discovered hard currency notes are less than 5 million yuan, and the China and Jiaotong Commercial Banks' banknotes total approximately 5 million yuan. Combined with the 12 million yuan of hard currency raised by the mint, the total circulating throughout the province is only 70 million yuan in hard currency and banknotes. The province's population has now increased to more than 13 million, and prices are high (except for grain prices), far exceeding those of the past. The need for goods and mediums of exchange (currency) should naturally increase accordingly. However, the Official Silver Bank has always been extremely cautious about issuing more banknotes, fearing that it would affect its credit. Although there have been proposals to allow the various counties to issue commercial stickers or circulating notes, it is ultimately felt that there are many drawbacks and they are hesitant to try it lightly. Therefore, after a full vote, it was decided to suggest to the authorities that several tens of millions of yuan of prize-winning bonds be issued to provide farmers and merchants with capital for turnover, to be fully redeemed in two years, with interest paid every six months. In order to strengthen credit, it was decided to invite the Liaoning Banking Group and the leaders of various legal entities to join in order to show openness. It was generally agreed to elect Lu Muting, the Director of the Dongsan Province Official Silver Bank, and Jin Enqi, the President of the General Chamber of Commerce, to represent them in meeting with Zang Shiyi, the Chairman of the Provincial Government, to explain everything in detail and request approval for implementation (20th).

Taishun was captured by bandits in September, and the magistrate disappeared. The provincial government then appointed Ma Chengji, the former magistrate of Tongxiang County, to fill the position. Ma declined the appointment, and Xu Huhu was appointed instead. Xu has not yet taken office. According to a report submitted by the Taishun fellows association in Hangzhou, they are asking for rapid relief to the suffering people after the bandit disaster. The provincial government ordered Magistrate Xu to take office quickly to handle post-disaster affairs.

The Xiaochang Light Railway, from Xixing to Zhuji, spans more than 100 li. The earthwork, bridge, and culvert projects are expected to be completed in January of the 20th year of the Republic (1931). The Jianshan Bridge, which is related to farmland irrigation, has also been ordered to be rebuilt and perfected. It is also scheduled to open to traffic on March 1 of the 20th year of the Republic (1931), making Hangzhou and Zhuji instantly accessible.

Yang Shijie, the inspector of the County Public Security Bureau and the head of the inspection office, uncovered a major theft at the home of Hu Aquan in Dawuqiao today (24th) afternoon, recovering more than 20 stolen items. The case involved thefts from the County Normal School and the homes of Wang in Beimen, Wang behind Puzhao Temple, and Yan in Xinei. The case has been transferred for investigation.

Lüxiang, Jinshan County, Suffers Three Robberies. Lüxiang Town, Jinshan County, previously suffered revenge after the chief of the public security sub-bureau arrested a certain major bandit, resulting in the murder of the chief of the public security sub-bureau, Chief Jiang, and widespread looting. Now, it has been robbed twice more. In the last robbery on the night of the 19th of this month, even the more substantial shops were not spared, resulting in losses of tens of thousands of yuan. Now that the Fifth Division of the Army has dispatched troops to station in the town, people's hearts have begun to settle down.

Suzhou 77

Three Bandits Executed by Firing Squad: The First and Second Districts of the Water Police successively captured Pu Tongsheng and Wang Desheng, the main culprits in the kidnapping case of Chen Peizhi of Meiyan, and Shen Laohu, the main culprit in the kidnapping case of Cao Wenying of Damiaogang. They were handed over to the Wujiang County Government for trial. They were all sentenced to death and approved by the Provincial Government. On the afternoon of the 23rd, they were taken to the execution ground outside Dongmen in Wujiang for execution by firing squad.

Surplus Public Bond Funds Allocated to Reformatory Expenses: The Wuxian Relief Institute and Reformatory for Vocational Training need more than 15,500 yuan for expenses this year, but the income is only a little over 2,000 yuan, a huge discrepancy. Therefore, the Relief Institute sent a letter to the County Government requesting the Storage Committee to provide subsidies to maintain operations. Local gentry are also very concerned about the institute's expenses and plan to allocate the surplus of over 30,000 yuan from Wuxian public bonds to the institute's expenses. A proposal has been prepared and submitted to the Third County Administrative Conference for discussion.

Robbery and Assault in Yinshan Township: On the 23rd, more than twenty bandits suddenly came to the homes of Ye Wenming, Wu Fuying, Zhang Huijin, and Shen Huisheng in Nanbang Village, Yinshan Township, Su County, and robbed them separately. They also burned Zhou, the wife of Shen Huisheng, on her left arm with candles. The loss was about 500 yuan. A report has been filed for arrest.

Second Joint Defense Conference of Four Counties: The joint defense offices of Wuxian, Wujiang, Qingpu, and Kunshan counties were established in Suzhou. The inaugural meeting and the second joint defense conference were held in Suzhou on the afternoon of the 24th. Huang Yunzhen from Wuxian, Wu Jia from Wujiang, Pang Shusen from Kunshan, and Yu Ding from Qingpu attended. Huang Yunzhen presided over the meeting and approved the organizational rules of the joint defense offices of the four counties and decided on joint defense measures before adjourning.

Hengjing: Robbery of Farmhouses: On the evening of the 23rd, bandits suddenly came to the homes of Shen Hongru, Shen Laotai, and Shen Yinshi in Beitang Village, Hengjing, and robbed them with weapons. The loss was more than 400 yuan. The county police team has been reported to for investigation of the stolen goods and arrest of the bandits.

Opening Traffic and Demolishing Archways: After the development of Guanqian Street, it has not been opened to traffic because the sidewalks on both sides have not been built. Now that the sidewalk problem has been solved, the county government has decided to resume traffic on December 1st. Furthermore, the screen walls of the Jixiang and Ruyi gates have been ordered by the provincial government to be demolished. The Ministry of Interior also ordered the Civil Affairs Department to instruct the county government that the stone archway in Gongxiang Lane is not a famous historical site and obstructs the road. The owners are advised to demolish it voluntarily immediately.

Wuxi 78

County Court Scheduled to be Established: Since the Higher Court appointed Yao Guozhang, the chief of the Wuxi County Court Preparatory Office, and Wang Yi, the clerk of the First Civil Court, to come to Wuxi, they have been actively preparing with County Magistrate Pan. The Judicial Progress Association and the silk and yarn industries have been responsible for raising the opening expenses and repairing the housing expenses. The funds have been raised in advance and construction is underway. The Higher Court has prepared a regular budget and submitted it to the Provincial Government for submission to the Provincial Government Committee for review by the Department of Finance. It has been approved to be changed to 1,400 yuan per month. Lin Biao, the president of the Higher Court, has decided that January 1, 20th year, will be the official date for the establishment of the Wuxi County Court. The candidate for the president of the court has not yet been determined, but the court building will be completed soon. President Lin has appointed Director Yao to come to Wuxi to inspect and accept it.

Urgent Progress in Building the Ring Road Around the Lake: The provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang plan to build a ring road around Taihu Lake. In Jiangsu Province, it will pass through the three counties of Wuxi, Suzhou, and Wujiang, with a total length of 130 kilometers. The entire road survey was completed at the end of this month. The main products along the line are rice, wheat, silk, and cocoons, and the mountains along the lake are especially famous for their fruits. The Department of Construction has decided to start construction on the section within Jiangsu Province at the beginning of next month because of the important commercial relationship of this road.

Telegram Requesting Postponement of Wheat Inspection Office: The Ministry of Agriculture and Mining established a wheat inspection office in Shanghai to handle wheat inspection matters. Shanghai has already implemented it early and sent Gu Leshan to Wuxi to negotiate the establishment of an inspection branch immediately. The Rice and Bean Industry Association believes that this matter is of great importance to the interests of the industry. After repeated discussions by the association, it was agreed that Wuxi is an inland city and its nature is different from that of Shanghai. It was decided to send a letter to the Chamber of Commerce to forward it to the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining to postpone its implementation. The Chamber of Commerce has already telegraphed the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining yesterday to request a postponement.

Bandits Send Letters to Extort Huge Sums: Demao Shen Silk and Satin Shop in Meichang Lane outside the North Gate of Xiyi is solely owned by Shen Jinhua, a local. It has been in business for decades and is doing well. The other day, Shen Jinhua suddenly received a letter from bandits borrowing 50,000 yuan for military expenses and setting a deadline for payment. After receiving the letter, Shen knew that it was an extortion attempt by bandits and ignored it.

Water Patrol Team Captures Thieves and Escorts Them to Xiyi for Interrogation: Qian Tianxiong, captain of the Xiyi Water Patrol Team, recently received a tip that thieves who had repeatedly robbed ships in Qingcheng City and other places were hiding in the British Concession in Shanghai. After receiving the report, Captain Qian met with Liao Dajin, the leader of the Detective Team of the Police Brigade, the day before yesterday afternoon, and took a car to Shanghai to report to the British Concession Police Station. The police chief dispatched several detectives to assist in the arrest. They captured Gu Rongxing, the main culprit, near Mantingfang and escorted him back to Xiyi last night. Captain Qian interrogated him severely. Gu confessed to having many accomplices. According to his confession, Qian immediately escorted him to the county government for interrogation.

Daughter-in-Law Abused and Committed Suicide: Ji Ziqiu, a rude and violent villager in Houzao Village near Yuqi Town, District 15 (Qingcheng City) of the county, is currently serving as the chief of the 83rd Tu. His son, A Jin, married Xu Shundi, the daughter of Xu Aqi from Xutianli Xujia Village, in the 15th year of the Republic of China through a matchmaker. After entering the house, she was often abused by her father-in-law, Ji Ziqiu. The other day, Ziqiu was eager to raise money for money matters, so he asked his daughter-in-law, Shundi, for money. When he failed, he roared and cursed. After being abused, Shundi suddenly had a pessimistic view of life and hanged herself in the room secretly last night. By the time it was discovered the next day, she had already died. After someone reported it, the parents of the deceased, Xu Aqi and his wife, rushed to Ji's house after hearing the news and cried loudly over the body. On the one hand, they prepared to have serious negotiations with Ji Ziqiu and reported to the 15th Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau to request that Ji Ziqiu be detained and dealt with according to the law.

Changzhou 79

Changzhou-Jiangyin Ships Robbed: A ship sailing from Changzhou to Jiangyin set sail from Changzhou the night before last with a total of more than thirty passengers. When passing near Yangtou Bridge, seven or eight bandits suddenly boarded the ship with guns and arbitrarily searched all the ship owners and passengers. All the hidden money was robbed, and they fired a shot to leave with the stolen goods after about an hour.

Provincial Government Approves Additional Levy of Mu Tax: The local expenses for the 18th and 19th years of Wuyi County were insufficient. The county government convened a temporary administrative conference to decide to levy an additional 1.5 li of mu tax to make up for the shortfall. The county government's finance bureau submitted it to the finance department, which forwarded it to the provincial government for approval. It is learned that the provincial government has approved the additional levy in the second half of the 19th year.

Jiangyin 80

Chengxi-Min to Establish Long-Distance Telephone: The Ministry of Communications believes that long-distance telephones are more convenient than telegraphs. In addition to the Suzhou-Changshu branch line, which has been completed, the Yixing-Wuxi-Jiangyin section of the Beijing-Shanghai trunk line is under construction. Recently, the Suzhou Telegraph Bureau was ordered to prepare and send personnel to Cheng to contact Yan Jiatong, director of the Jiangyin Telegraph Bureau, to investigate the telephone bureau's situation so that the problems of future telephone connection can be implemented. The lines will be set up on the existing telegraph poles with the available funds.

Chen Wanfeng Safely Escaped Danger: Chen Wanfeng from Zhouzhuang went to Liyang to collect rent the other day and was kidnapped by bandits. His son, Chen Qiucha (district chief of the 12th district), went to Liyang after receiving the news. His father had safely escaped danger. He had been kidnapped for four days. He didn't lose much money because the bandits learned that Chen was not rich, so they released him.

Water Police Captain Compiles and Checks Ships: Shen Hualong, the captain of the 20th Brigade of the Water Public Security Team, has decided to compile and check the local and foreign merchant ships coming and going from each port from December 1st due to the winter defense period and the unstable bandit atmosphere in the north and south of the Yangtze River, as well as the confusing variety of ships entering and exiting the ports. Licenses will be issued to provide a basis for investigation.

The Issue of Closing the 25th Rear Hospital: Since the military has settled down and the north and south are unified, the general headquarters has ordered the closure of rear hospitals in various places. The Jiangyin 25th Rear Hospital has been established for several months. The general hospital is in Shifang Lane outside the South Gate, and the branch is in the Chengzun Middle School in the city. Zhang Gongshi and other cadres of the school's autonomous association have described the difficulties in finding accommodation for students after the school building was borrowed by the hospital, and have requested relief. However, according to a certain military doctor, the issue of closing the rear hospital in Jiangyin still needs time and must wait until the closure of various places is completed, or it may be postponed for three months. However, it has not yet been determined whether the hospital site will be set up elsewhere.

Xing Songwen and Others Will Be Escorted to Suzhou Within Days: Xing Songwen, the former district chief of the First District, Xu Yan, the assistant district chief, Zhou Qiujiang, a member of the Chamber of Commerce, and Xu Awu, a resident of Dongwai (who sent rural newspapers to the People's and Commercial News Agency), were arrested with Ji Hehua, Cai Rushan, and others in September for reactionary cases. They have been detained and escorted for several months. Li County Magistrate recently reported to the Provincial Government, which instructed that Ji Hehua and Cai Rushan had been escorted to the Provincial Military Law Association for interrogation and handling, while Xing Songwen and the other three were under the jurisdiction of the Higher Court. After receiving the order, Li County Magistrate will send personnel to Suzhou within days.

Changshu 81

All Hostages in Nian Shao Bridge Kidnapping Case Escape Danger: It is learned that the family of Qu Shangzhen of Nianbu Bridge, Dongwu District, of this county, a total of six people, who were kidnapped by bandits, were hidden by the bandits in a den in Ren'an Port and extorted 30,000 yuan to redeem them. Qu repeatedly negotiated with the bandit leader and was allowed to reduce it to 3,800 yuan, with a limit of one week, otherwise they would tear up the ticket. After the conditions were agreed upon, the bandits first sent Qu Shangzhen by boat to the beach in Fushan District to land. When he landed, it was night and the place where he parked was far from the shore. Qu waded ashore. After returning home, he sold the farmland and asked powerful people to go by boat. It is said that the Qu family has now escaped danger and returned home, spending a total of more than 4,000 yuan.

Yangzhou 82

Autopsy to Verify the Corpse's Identity: It is learned that Kong Xianshi, a resident of Gujia Village, Shaobo, of this county, was shot and killed on the way to his cousin Xiankai's house for drinking. Now it is learned that the deceased's sons, Qingtong and Qingyan, his wife, Guo, his nephew, Qingfu, his grandson, Fanbin, his son-in-law, Shi Enyi, and his daughter, Kong Daguniang, and others believe that Xianshi's life and death are unknown and have learned that Xiankai is suspected of being the mastermind because Kai and Shi had fought over the position of township director. Fearing that he would hold a grudge and poison him, the family members filed a lawsuit with the county court, arrested Xiankai, and submitted it to the Higher Court to extend an invitation to Wang Yuanchen, the director of the Zhenjiang Provincial Hospital, together with Zhu Deming, the director of chemical inspection, Xue Wenyong, and other doctors, more than ten people, to come to Yangzhou yesterday morning (the 24th) at 10 o'clock out of Quekou City at Chi Tuo Temple to open the coffin and inspect it according to law. After the inspection, according to Wang Yuanchen's report, it was found that the deceased had two gunshots in his body, with gunshot wounds and a lot of congestion in the intestines, and there were no signs of poisoning on the skin, bones, and various key parts. It was indeed a gunshot wound that caused his death.

Execution of a Soldier Who Incited Soldiers: The headquarters of the 133rd Brigade stationed in Yangzhou reported that two soldiers, Zhang Zijin and Tao Shoushan, of the machine gun company of the First Battalion of the 265th Regiment, incited soldiers to plot disobedience. The headquarters sentenced Tao Shoushan to one year of imprisonment and Zhang Zijin to death. Therefore, the prisoner was escorted to the Huayou Institute execution ground at 3 pm today (the 22nd) for execution by firing squad.

Continued Report on the Robbery and Assault of Police Officers by Opium Offenders: It is learned that Liao, the inspector of the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau of Guazhou County, led more than ten armed police officers to investigate and arrest the suspects yesterday (the 21st) after four patrol officers from the bureau discovered opium offenders in Huojia Bridge the other day, and were robbed by a crowd of people in the area and assaulted. However, after arriving in the town, all the arrested opium offenders had escaped without a trace, making it impossible to arrest them. The inspector immediately returned to the city to report and sent the injured police officers Mo Ying, Chen Guoquan, Zhou Daoxian, and Ji Hengfu to the court for injury examination.

Jiaxing 83

The Victim Was Stolen and Drowned While Chasing: Ma Wenrong, 19 years old, from Tangnan, Jiaoshanmen Bridge, Jiaxing, was studying at Qiaoshe Primary School in the city. He returned home for recuperation due to illness. Unexpectedly, late at night the other day, his grandmother, Ma Shen, and grandson, Ma Wenrong, were both sleeping when they heard the sound of footsteps on the wall, knowing it was bandits. The grandmother and grandson avoided separately. Later, the bandits broke into the house with knives and sticks and searched separately. They found Ma Wenrong in the Long Kang and ordered him to point out where the silver was hidden. They even tied him up and beat him. After handing over 27 yuan, the bandits were still not satisfied. At this time, Wenrong took them by surprise and slipped out of the gate. However, the house faced the river on both sides, and the river was guarded by bandits. The bandits behind him had already tracked him down, and Wenrong waded into the water to escape, but drowned because he did not know how to swim. However, all the bandits spoke with a Henan accent, and Ma Shen was afraid of retaliation in the future, so she refused to give their names.

A Case of Murdering One's Own Husband Discovered in Xinshe City: Cao, a woman from Xinshe City, Jiaxing, had Ma Shunbao recruited as her son-in-law by her mother two years ago. However, the woman had fallen in love with Zhou Fuguan from the same village early on. After Ma Shunbao was recruited, he only knew how to work in the fields and rarely lived with Cao, so Cao still made excuses to go out and meet Zhou secretly. Recently, Ma Shunbao's uncle learned of the secret and told Cao that if she did not change her ways, he would send her to the authorities for investigation. Cao discussed with Zhou to murder Shunbao. After the plan was decided, on a certain day the other day, they strangled Shunbao to death and sank his body in the nearby river. However, the circumstances of the murder were seen by Cao's younger brother, who was afraid that he would also be harmed and did not dare to speak out. Afterwards, he told the clansmen, Cao Wu, who in turn told the village head, Chen Tiande, who told the village chief, Bai Yinxiang. The Yuxian Public Security Bureau arrested the murderers Cao and Zhou Fuguan. After being interrogated by Director Ying, and confirmed by Cao's brother, they confessed to the crime. Yesterday, the witnesses were escorted to the court for investigation. They were ordered to be guarded. Yesterday, Prosecutor Shen led the inspection officials to open the coffin and examine Ma Shunbao's body.

Pinghu 84

Xu Shuru Dies Tragically in the Line of Duty: Xu Shuru, a native of this county, lives in Xincang Town in the eastern part of the county and is currently the chief of the Jingkou Station Police Section. The special express train from Pingnan to the south returned from Hanbei at 12 pm on the 12th. When passing a certain place six li south of Jingkou, Xu and Leng Changyu, a clerk from the document section, were traveling south from Jingkou by handcar. It was already 7:30 pm. The handcar did not have a light, so they collided with each other. Xu and Leng were both crushed to death at the same time, and their bodies were a bloody mess, a terrible sight. Xu and Leng had been in public service for many years, and the road bureau colleagues asked the authorities to provide generous compensation.

Oil Ship Encountered Robbery: An oil ship drifted to the sea off Zhapu. The ship was full of kerosene, but it had no anchor or rudder. It was found that the ship was loaded with 260 large oil cans, which were the goods of the Shanghai Mei Da Company being shipped to the Hangzhou Branch. The ship, named Ni Hongxing, encountered danger at Wangjia Pass. The ship's anchor and rudder were destroyed by thieves and drifted to Zhapu and stranded. The company was notified to send personnel to inspect the goods. It is rumored that the company has sent personnel to Zhapu to negotiate.

Huzhou 85

Three Villages Near the City Were Robbed at the Same Time: On the night of the 20th, at about 2:00 am, seven or eight bandits, each carrying guns and weapons and speaking with a Henan accent, suddenly arrived at Shen Aji's house in Qianzhuang Village, District 1, Baimeiwei, outside the North Gate of this city, only a few miles from the city, and broke into the house. Aji heard the alarm and escaped first. The bandits entered and arbitrarily searched, looting all the clothes, silks, and cotton, causing a loss of more than 200 yuan. Shen Aji's elder brother, Zengfu, was shot in the head by the bandits. At the same time, in Panzhu Village in the same district, more than ten bandits, each carrying pistols and flashlights, first went to the house of Sun, the village chief, and rammed the door. Fortunately, the door and walls of the house were strong and could not be broken. The bandits broke into the house of Wang, Sun's left neighbor, and carried out a large-scale robbery. A large amount of clothes and ornaments were robbed. Also in the same district, in Xinglong Village, at about 3:00 am on the same night, more than ten bandits speaking with a Yu accent, each carrying guns, knives, and sticks, suddenly arrived at the village. They first fired a shot to show their strength and then went to rob three families, including the Wu family. The loss of the three families was about 500 yuan.

Security Team Rescues a Large Number of Hostages: The bandit situation in Changxing and other areas of Huzhou has become more rampant recently, so the troops stationed in Changxing are paying close attention to patrolling the area day and night. The other day, soldiers from the security team were patrolling when they suddenly encountered a large group of forty or fifty bandits in the Yaojia Bridge area. The two sides immediately opened fire and fought for an hour. The bandits were overwhelmed and gradually retreated. Several bandits were killed on the spot and four were captured alive, and seventeen hostages of all sizes were rescued. They were brought back to the team for interrogation. In addition to the hostages being kept in the team for claiming, the four bandits who were captured have been escorted to the headquarters of the Second Regiment of the Security Team in this city for verification and handling.

Fengxian 86

Announcement of the Reorganized Committee of the Relief Institute: This county's Relief Institute was established in October of the 18th year. All the members were self-elected from the directors of the original charitable organizations. However, for a year, it has been procrastinating and unable to be established. Wang Bo, the district chief of the Third District, and others raised questions. Therefore, it was decided to reorganize at the last local temporary meeting and stipulated the number of committee members, which was handed over to County Magistrate Shen to select. Zhang Xinjian (Party), Jiang Qingfan (County Government), Chen Beiyi, Tang Yunsheng, Wang Mengpei (incumbent committee members re-elected), Zhuang Qingqi, Ruan Xiyao, Zhu Ganye, and Jiang Rongchu (local gentry) were appointed to serve as seven people. It has been submitted to the Ministry of Civil Affairs for approval and filing. Therefore, the county government officially hired them yesterday and held a meeting in Nanqiao to establish it.

The Director of the Education Bureau Officially Takes Over: Since Song Binggong was appointed as the director of the Education Bureau of this county by the provincial government, the education community has had a welcome and rejection issue. Fortunately, those who advocate it are only a minority and their opinions are divided, so it has not been expanded and has been eliminated invisibly. At the same time, there are also those who have telegraphed to welcome the new director. It is learned that Song Ren has arrived in Nanqiao at 10 am yesterday and will go to the public place this morning to officially take over.

Important News 87

Hangzhou City Educational Institutions Implement New Budget

Totaling More Than 335,000 Yuan Annually

From the 19th year, Hangzhou City Education originally intended to actively expand. After deliberation, the municipal government formulated an expansion plan and budget, totaling 366,607.9 yuan. The Department of Education gave a reduction of 20,828.7 yuan, changing it to 335,779.2 yuan. Three new grades were added to the municipal junior high school, ten new grades were added to the municipal elementary school in the first semester, and twenty-seven new grades will be added in the second semester. A total of thirty-seven new grades were added to the elementary school. It is heard that the municipal government has issued notices to all educational institutions in the city, informing them that the expenses of all educational institutions in the city will be implemented in accordance with the new budget from August of this year, as the budget has been approved by the Department of Education and submitted to the provincial government.

Jiang Menglin Plans to Establish a Yuyao County Middle School 88

Jiang Menglin, in view of the fact that there are more than 300 elementary school graduates in his hometown of Yuyao every year, but no junior high school has been established, specially initiated the establishment of a junior high school with local gentry. Women's Political and Legal Training School Welcomes School Board Members 90

The Capital Women's Political and Legal Training School held a meeting yesterday (the 22nd) to welcome school board members Yu Zhizhen and Wang Xiaozhen. School board member Jiao Yitang and Principal Long Jiujing hosted the event. About 200 faculty, staff, and students of the entire school attended. Local

Liu Zhanen and Others Will Issue a Statement Asking the Municipal Council to Investigate Schools 92

The Investigation Is Based on a Letter from the Chinese Ratepayers Association

丨Ministry of Education Translation Name Will Change丨

Guo Wen She reported that the Shanghai Concession Municipal Council recently issued a letter to investigate schools in the concession in the name of the Education Department. People in this city have repeatedly expressed opposition to this move in newspapers. It has been found that the motivation of the Municipal Council for this move was based on a clause in a letter from the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Shanghai Concession on March 26th of the 17th year of the Republic of China ("Under the current situation, the responsibility of expanding Chinese education in the concession should be emphasized"). Therefore, the Education Committee of the Design Agency was organized this year. The committee name is Ｂｏａｒｄ　ｏｆ　Ｅｄｕｏａｔｉｏｎ, with three Chinese members, namely Liu Zhanen and others, as well as four Westerners and one Japanese. Mr. Liu believes that under the current situation, there are too many students who drop out of school in the concession, and it is imperative to promote education so that Chinese education in the concession gradually becomes consistent with national education. However, to promote education, it is necessary to first clarify the current situation of education in the concession before there is a basis. This is the origin of the publication of the investigation. As for the Municipal Council issuing a letter to investigate in the name of the Education Department, it was not a resolution of the Education Committee, nor was it something that other gentlemen had ever heard of. Because the Municipal Council originally had an Education Department (Ｅｄｕｃａｔｉｏｎ　Ｄｅｔａｒｌｍｅｎｔ), those who translated it into Chinese used the word "Department" because the Chinese names of the Municipal Council's police, health, and other agencies all used the word "Department", so it was translated as "Department". After this matter was discovered, Mr. Liu and others thought it was inappropriate and proposed to change it. It will soon be changed. Mr. Liu and others will also issue an advertisement to answer all sectors of the community concerned about education in the concession.

County Education Bureau Meeting Minutes 93

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 176th bureau meeting yesterday after the weekly memorial service. Attendees included Bureau Chief Shi, Zheng Guoqi, Sun Tingfang, Lin Weiwen, Niu Zhiyi, Yang Huiming, Yan Chongguang, Yao Jue, Xi Siwu, Cai Xingsan, Zhu Xixue, Wu Renyuan, and Pan Xingsan. Bureau Chief Shi presided, and Pan Xingsan served as recorder. The meeting followed established protocol. Matters reported were omitted. Discussion items: (1) Regarding the proposal from the Second District Office to appoint nearby village chiefs as school property custodians for village primary schools, a matter that had already been approved in principle by the bureau-district conference, the discussion focused on determining the title and regulations for implementation. The resolution was to note that, according to the Law on Village Autonomy, the village chief already has the responsibility to handle education and other cultural matters, and therefore, there was no need to establish a separate title. The intention of the original proposal was largely commendable, and it was resolved to have Education Commissioners Lin and Niu draft implementation regulations for further discussion at a future meeting. (2) Regarding the issue of the Municipal Land Bureau issuing a topographical map of the county temple property to the bureau, showing a shortage of approximately three acres compared to the original records, the resolution was to send a letter to the Municipal Land Bureau inquiring about the following points: A. How much land was taken for road construction? B. How much was deducted for the Lake Heart Pavilion and the river? And what other reasons were there for the discrepancy? (3) Regarding the school equipment survey forms that had been reviewed and revised, a discussion was held. The resolution was to approve the forms and instruct that they be distributed to the schools for completion. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Jiangnan College Welcomes New Board Members 94

Jiangnan College held a reception two days ago (the 22nd) to welcome the school's Chairman of the Board, Ye Kaixin, and invited board members, guests, and the entire faculty and student body, numbering in the hundreds. Ling Xianwen presided, with Jiang Zirong and Cao Lunfang as recorders, and Liu Zhuqing as master of ceremonies. The chairman delivered a welcoming speech, followed by Chairman Ye's address, stating that he would take full responsibility for the school and hoped that all students would study diligently and contribute to society and bring glory to the nation in the future. Following him, board members translated and exchanged remarks from Li Fengting, Wu Shaoxian, Guo Yuanjue, and others. The event concluded at 5:00 PM with a group photograph.

Shanghai Art College to Hold Three Ceremonies 95

The Shanghai Art College has been established for nineteen years. Recently, several new buildings have been added and completed. Furthermore, the alumni association is holding its founding meeting. Therefore, the college authorities, in collaboration with student organizations, have established a grand preparatory committee to celebrate. Currently, the entire school is focused on preparing substantial academic and artistic performances. It has been decided to hold the alumni association founding meeting on the 27th of this month, a concert on the evening of the 27th, and the 19th-anniversary celebration of the college's founding and the inauguration of the new buildings on the morning of the 28th. Authorities from various organizations, reporters from newspapers, and renowned scholars will be invited to deliver speeches. Moreover, from the 28th to the 30th, the college will hold an exhibition of this semester's achievements for three days to showcase the school's efforts in academics. This will be complemented by various recreational activities such as Peking opera, spoken drama, Kunqu opera, magic, and humorous skits, crosstalk, and dances. The school has over six hundred students.

Results of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Private Middle School Football Tournament: Shanghai College Wins the Championship 96

Defeated Jinling Yesterday with a Score of Four to One

Huilan and Jinling Tie for Second Place

The final match of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Private Middle School Athletic Association's football championship was held in Yangshupu for several days. Shanghai College and Jinling College reached the final and competed for the championship at 10:00 AM yesterday. Shanghai College defeated Jinling with a score of four to one, and Shanghai College won the championship. The consolation final was also held at 10:00 AM yesterday, with Huilan defeating Soochow University with a score of three to zero. Huilan and Jinling were originally scheduled to play for second place tomorrow, but because both teams had to return to their schools last night, the match was moved to 3:00 PM yesterday, resulting in a 1-1 tie, and both teams shared the second-place position. Hu Minmin was the referee for the game. A brief account of the championship match is given below.

Both Shanghai College and Jinling College had many talented players, and each victory was hard-won. In the final, both teams were determined to seize the championship, so the battle was fierce. Shanghai College's unity and coordination were effective. Center forward Dai Linzhen had the spirit of his elder brother Linjing, lively and strong, and scored the first goal. Jinling tried to advance and exact revenge. The goal of Shanghai College was heavily guarded. Shanghai College committed two penalty kicks within twenty yards, but Jinling only scored on one of them, resulting in a 1-1 tie at halftime.

In the second half, Shanghai College's discipline was strict, and their attacks were even more aggressive. Although Jinling tried its best to resist, they suffered from fatigue. There were many opportunities to attack, but Shanghai College's comprehensive defense left no chance. Shanghai College launched a large-scale offensive. The defense was tight, and the forwards scored with all their might. Li Ruchun, Jing Yong, and Lin Guanghua all scored goals, achieving a resounding victory of four to one. Xu Zhendong was the referee. The lineups of both teams were as follows:

A Fierce Battle Between Chung Hua and Pirates 100

Chung Hua's inside guards, Liao Lie and Guan Yi, were skilled and good at defense, and Liao Lie's skills were particularly outstanding. With these two generals, Chung Hua's defense was as solid as a city wall. The three forwards, Chen Baoqiu, He Yanzhang, and Wei Zuohan, also cooperated well. Tou Ren then scored another free throw, leaving the two teams separated by one point. Under the supervision of Liao and Guan, the Pirates could not move freely and paused the game to discuss countermeasures and continue fighting. The Pirates' formation was indeed good, but their shooting was poor, and they only scored one goal in several throws. However, Chen soon caught up, and the two teams fought fiercely. The first half ended in a 9-9 tie. In the second half, Tafel threw the ball into the basket under the basket. Chung Hua's Yan Furui also scored from the crowd. The Pirates then relied on Tou Ren's strength to add three points. Chung Hua's inside guards Liao and Guan participated in the attack one after another, and Yan also scored one point, putting Chung Hua ahead with 17 to 14. The Pirates, unable to score with close shots, tried long-range shots. With the blessing of the gods, Pike and Tou Ren both succeeded. In the last four minutes, Zhu Kaiming replaced Yan and scored a free throw as soon as he entered the field, tying the score at 18. Then, Liao of Chung Hua and Lao of Pirates each scored a long-range shot, making the score 20. At this critical moment, the referee acted arbitrarily. Pirates relied on Pike's goal to win by luck with a score of 22 to 20. The referee was Bates.

Madam Zhang Xueliang, Yu Fengzhi, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 116

Arrived with Mr. and Mrs. Zhang Xueming

Because She Needs to Accompany the Deputy Commander to the North

She Will Return to Beijing Before Friday of This Week

The Trip to Hangzhou Was Too Hasty and Was Cancelled

Madam Yu Fengzhi, wife of Zhang Xueliang, and Mr. and Mrs. Zhang Xueming, Director of the Tianjin Public Security Bureau and younger brother of Zhang Xueliang, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at dawn. When the special train arrived at the station, the sound of the whistle could be heard from afar. Those welcoming them stood smiling and waiting for the special train to enter the platform. At 6:40 AM, with the wheels rolling, music played on the platform and the crowd surged forward. Many people in military uniforms leaned out of the train windows and nodded to the welcomers. A photographer from this newspaper immediately took her picture

Portrait of Madam Yu Fengzhi (Photo by Ye Changlie) 117

To Commemorate the Occasion, Madam Zhang was wearing a sky-blue cheongsam with a black overcoat with a fur collar. Her demeanor was calm and her face was cheerful. Madam Yu seemed to enjoy the scenery of the Jiangnan region.

People Who Arrived Together: In addition to Mr. and Mrs. Zhang Xueming, those who accompanied Madam Yu Fengzhi included the Mayor of Qingdao, Hu Ruoyu, the Director of the Tianjin Second Special District, Ning Xiangnan, the Deputy Director of the Sipingtaonan Railway Bureau, Mr. and Mrs. Wu Jingan, the Secretary and Madam Shen Zutong, the British advisor to the Northeast Commander, Mr. Yagg, the President of the Tianjin Court, Du Zexian, the Secretary Zhao Yunpu, the Medical Officer Wu Xiaolou, the Adjutants Wang, Zhang, and Zhao, and sixteen staff members. Soldiers, police, and detectives were at the station providing tight security.

Breakfast at Rongpu: After getting off the train, Madam Yu Fengzhi and Mr. and Mrs. Zhang Xueming drove to Chen's Rongpu at 243 Haig Road to rest. Madam Yu was in Chen Diaoyuan's No. 797 sedan car. The cars that followed numbered over twenty, snaking along the road. The cars arrived at Rongpu around 7:00 AM. The Zhangs went inside to rest, while Zhang Xueming met with guests in the main hall. Mr. Zhang's face was fuller than Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang's. He was wearing a gray-brown robe with a black mandarin jacket and a black short outer jacket. Judging from his remarks, he was very optimistic.

Portrait of Mr. Zhang Xueming (Photo by Ye Changlie) 118

The small photo included is the one taken in the main hall of Rongpu. The rest of the entourage stayed at the Cangzhou Hotel.

Yu Fengzhi's Remarks: After Madam Yu Fengzhi and her party arrived at Rongpu, a reporter from this newspaper also drove there to pay a visit. We were granted an audience. Madam Zhang said that she had two missions for her trip to Shanghai: (1) Deputy Commander originally planned to take the time to visit Shanghai and Hangzhou during this trip south. Now, because matters in Beijing had not been completed and he was eager to return north, the trip to Shanghai and Hangzhou was cancelled. I am here to thank everyone on behalf of the Deputy Commander for their warm welcome. (2) In the past, I was in charge of fundraising for the disaster relief in western Liaoning. I am grateful to all sectors of Shanghai for their generous support and the huge amount of funds raised, which greatly benefited the disaster victims. Therefore, I came to Shanghai to thank all sectors on behalf of the disaster victims. I also visited the Women's Association and the Women's Political and Legal College in Beijing and found the various facilities to be excellent models. I will make efforts to promote women's education in the future when I return to Liaoning to ensure that men and women are equal in learning and ability.

Zhang Xueming's Remarks: The reporter then met with Zhang Xueming. Reporter: What is your impression of this trip south? Zhang: The capital is full of vitality, everything is being renewed, and the future of the country is promising. However, I am engaged in police affairs, so I paid a lot of attention to police affairs in Beijing. The police facilities in the capital are very energetic, and the police officers are also lively, loyal, and diligent, which is commendable. However, the streets of Nanjing are too narrow, and it seems dangerous and difficult to rescue in case of a fire. Also, most of the ditches in Beijing are clogged, and there are too many ponds everywhere, which seems to be a bit lacking in terms of hygiene. Now it is planned to gradually improve, and the municipal administration will definitely be remarkable in the future. Reporter: What are your plans after arriving in Shanghai? Zhang: I plan to examine the police administration in the foreign concessions to learn from it. I heard that the police facilities in Hangzhou are very good, and I would like to go there for reference. Reporter: Will you return north by sea or by land? Zhang: The Deputy Commander will stay in Beijing for a few more days, but we must rush back to the capital before Friday of this week (the 28th) to accompany the Deputy Commander back north by train.

Yesterday's Activities: Around 9:00 AM yesterday, Mayor Zhang and his wife made a special trip to Rongpu to visit Madam Zhang and take care of everything. They had a very pleasant conversation. Then, they were invited to lunch at the Cangzhou Hotel. In the afternoon, they toured various places with Madam Zhang Qun and others. At 7:00 PM, Mr. and Mrs. Sun Ke and Chen Mingshu sent invitations to a banquet at the Xinghualou Restaurant to welcome more than 100 guests from all walks of life. After the banquet, Mr. and Mrs. Shen Nengyi accompanied Madam Zhang on a tour of the city.

Tonight's Grand Banquet: Madam Soong Mei-ling, wife of Chairman Chiang, originally intended to come with Madam Zhang, but she was unable to do so due to events, so she asked her sister, Madam Kong Xiangxi, Soong Ai-ling, to represent her. Mr. and Mrs. Kong Xiangxi will hold a banquet at their private residence today to welcome the Songhu Garrison Commander Xiong Shihui and Mr. and Mrs. Zhang. They will host a grand banquet at the Dahua Hotel at 8:00 PM to welcome more than 100 people, including Madam Tang Shaoyi, Madam Wellington Koo, and celebrities from all walks of life. After the banquet, there will be tea and dancing. The scene will be grand and lively.

Decision to Cancel the Hangzhou Tour: Madam Zhang, Zhang Xueming, and their party originally planned to take the opportunity to visit Hangzhou and see the sights of the Three Pagodas and Six Bridges. However, due to the limited time and the need to return to Beijing before Friday of this week (the 28th) to accompany Deputy Commander Zhang to the north, the tour of Hangzhou was canceled after detailed discussions last night between Madam Zhang and her aides.

Returning to Beijing Soon: This is Madam Zhang's first time in Shanghai, and she is very willing to do some sightseeing. However, according to news from this newspaper last night, there were plans to return to Beijing tonight, but various sectors have pleaded to stay. The itinerary may be delayed for a day or two. It is said that the facilities at Rongpu, where they are staying, are not very good. Today they may move to the Cathay Hotel on the Bund or the Sheng Residence on Jing'an Temple Road. Internal and External Debt Consolidation Meeting 119

Meeting held in Shanghai today

Minister Song and others arrive in Shanghai

Meeting focuses on discussions without ceremony

Representatives of Tianjin and Pingjin Banks arrive in Shanghai

The National Government's Internal and External Debt Consolidation Committee has held several meetings in Nanjing and announced the outline for consolidating foreign debt. It is now scheduled to continue the consolidation meeting in Shanghai starting today (25th), first discussing the plan for consolidating internal debt. Representatives of the Tianjin and Pingjin banking community's creditor group, including Zhou Zuomin, Tan Danya, Wang Zemin, and Zhu Yusheng, have successively arrived in Shanghai to report to the Ministry of Finance's office and handle meeting procedures. It is determined that representatives from the Shanghai banking community, including Zhang Gongquan, Ye Fuxiao, Hu Mengjia, Wu Yunzhai, Chen Zheqing, and Li Ming, will attend the meeting today. Many consolidation plans have been proposed in recent days. The National Government has also prepared to establish a fund and concrete consolidation policies, so the prices of various internal debts in the market have risen one after another. However, although today's meeting is held in the Ministry of Finance's office, it is said that because the meeting is of a discussion nature, there will be no ceremony, and news of the meeting will be kept secret for the time being to avoid affecting the market.

Another report states that the National Government's Internal and External Debt Consolidation Committee, presided over by Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance, has held several meetings in Nanjing. It is now scheduled to continue the meeting in Shanghai today. Minister Song intends to attend in person, so he came to Shanghai from Nanjing the day before yesterday. Zeng Rongfu, Secretary-General of the Internal and External Debt Consolidation Committee, also came with him and has been very busy preparing for the meeting in recent days. He will also attend the meeting today. Li Sihao, the newly appointed Chairman of the Internal and External Debt Consolidation Committee, also arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing last night and is scheduled to attend the meeting today and take office. It is said that Minister Song has been separately negotiating with ministers and chargés d'affaires of various countries on foreign debt consolidation methods and meeting dates in recent days.

Banking Community Organizes Internal Debt Creditor Group 120

Results of the Bankers Association meeting yesterday

Ten members nominated as initiators

Six representatives dispatched from Peiping by telegram to participate

Representatives from Pingjin arrive in Shanghai to establish group

The Shanghai banking community will discuss the consolidation of China's internal debt. After the banking sector's creditor group is established, a joint national registration of internal debt creditors will be held. The Shanghai Bankers Association convened a general membership meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Bankers Association at No. 4 Hong Kong Road for this matter. More than 20 managers from various banks attended. As a result of the discussion, ten members were nominated in Shanghai as initiators of the Chinese internal debt banking sector creditor group. The elected members include Li Fusun, Chairman of the Bank of China; Hu Mengjia, General Manager of the Bank of Communications; Wu Yunzhai, Manager of the Jin Cheng Bank; Ye Fuxiao, Manager of the Continental Bank; Chen Zheqing, Manager of the Y盐业 Bank; Hu Bijiang, Manager of the Zhongnan Bank; Sun Hengfu, Manager of the Siming Bank; Wang Xinguang, Manager of the Hongkou Commercial Bank; Chang Xiaobo, Manager of the Juxingcheng Bank; and Liu Huizhi of the China Industrial Bank. The Peiping Bankers Association sent a telegram yesterday nominating Zhang Gongquan, General Manager of the Bank of China; Lu Jianquan, Chairman of the Bank of Communications; Tan Danya, General Manager of the Continental Bank; Zhou Zuomin, Manager of the Jin Cheng Bank; Zhu Yusheng, Manager of the Peiping Y盐业 Bank; and Wang Zemin, Manager of the Peiping Baoshang Bank, as representatives to participate in the initiation. Except for Zhu Yusheng and Wang Zemin, who will arrive in Shanghai from Peiping within a few days, the other representatives are all in Shanghai, which is very convenient for consultation. However, the Tianjin Bankers Association had not yet replied by telegram as of last night, so a telegram has been sent again to inquire. It is expected that representatives will also come to Shanghai to participate within a few days. It is estimated that the various initiators in Shanghai will formally establish the internal debt creditor group as soon as the Pingjin representatives arrive to discuss the specific issues of internal debt consolidation. Then, all national creditors will register in full, and then a number of representatives will be re-elected from the creditor group to go to Nanjing to contact the Ministry of Finance and start the consolidation process.

After the End of Military Transportation, Jianghai Hualun Resumes Service 121

All routes will return to normal on the first of next month

Recent allocation of shipping is extremely busy

Due to the continuous domestic wars in the past two years, Jianghai Hualun has suspended service. This year, the Transportation Department rented as many as 70 merchant ships at its peak, allowing foreign ships to take the opportunity to become active. Domestic shipping companies have lost tens of millions in the transportation industry. By the end of September this year, the military operations ended, and many ships were returned. In October, in order to suppress the Communist bandits in Xiangjiang and Jiangxi, the military moved troops to the Yangtze River basin, and the Lu and Chen divisions changed their defenses to Anhui, so another 18 ships were rented for transportation. Now, the troops suppressing the bandits have reached their destination, and all the rented ships have been returned to Shanghai. The Jianghai ships, which had been suspended for a long time, have now fully resumed service. From December 1st, all Chinese merchant ships on the northern and southern oceans and the Yangtze River can resume their regular schedules. This is not only a turning point for the continuation of the shipping industry, but also an opportunity for the revival of national shipping. The various companies have been very busy planning the restoration and allocating routes in recent days, which is worth recording.

All Sea Vessels Return to Shanghai　Since the release of the Gongping, Xinchang, and Tangshan ships last week, only the Huayang and Tunan ships have not been released. Yesterday, when the China Merchants Bureau was preparing to report the charter fees for October and November, it telegraphed Nanjing to request the release of these two ships as soon as possible, as December 1st is the first day for the full resumption of regular schedules for national ships. It is heard that the Transportation Department has agreed to release the two sea vessels to Shanghai this month as a result of the charter procedures.

Four River Vessels to Return Immediately　At its peak, more than 20 Yangtze River ships were rented. Now, in addition to those that have been released, only the Jiangtian, Dexing, Fulong, Fengpu, and Xingshi ships remain. After repeated requests from Sanbei China Merchants to release the ships, they can return to Shanghai by the end of the month at the latest. Within the Yangtze River line, the Hualun ships have usually operated no more than six ships since last year, and they have been suspended and reopened from time to time. Now that the war has stopped and the ships have been released, and the navy is escorting them along the river, the China Merchants Bureau's Yangtze River ships can resume eight ships on the upper river, Sanbei can operate five ships on the upper river, and Ning Shao Zhaoxing can operate three ships, restoring the number of schedules before the war. The competition for cargo among the various companies has been very intense in recent days.

Beiyang to Resume Regular Schedules Immediately　The Beiyang regular schedule has been suspended for a long time. Now, although the China Merchants Bureau's Xinming has opened, the Xinfeng was hit by the Japanese ship Kageyama Maru and came to Shanghai for major repairs. Yesterday, it was confirmed that the losses for both goods and hull amounted to 40,000 yuan, and a claim has been filed with the Japanese Post Office and the Near Seas Association. The bureau plans to dispatch the Beiyang ships (1) Tianjin regular schedule: three ships: Xinfeng, Xinming, and Yushun (2) Dalian schedule: Tunan or Huayang (3) Haizhou schedule: Tonghua. The Nanhua ship is also scheduled to resume regular schedules on the 1st.

A List of All Ships Suspended from Service　From last year to the present, the length of time and the number of ships provided to the central government for rent are truly astonishing. The daily rental for each ship ranged from 300 yuan to 100 yuan. The rental fees for the past two years must have been several million yuan. The military transportation has ended, and the rental fees are being settled. The China Merchants Bureau alone has a considerable record of the dates of suspension of the various ships. The number of days of military transportation last year and the number of days of suspension as of September this year are recorded below, which can also give a glimpse of the situation.

Direct Express Train to Beijing and Liaoning Starts Yesterday 122

Circular from the Jinpu Railway Administration regarding train schedule

Circular from the Traffic Department of the Jinpu Railway Administration: In order to announce the matter, this road has decided to start a direct special express train for the Beijing-Liaoning joint transportation from November 24th. Two trains will run each week in both directions between Liaoning and Pukou. The down train will depart from Liaoning at 0:20 AM on Mondays and Fridays and arrive at Tianjin East Station at 8:00 PM that night. According to the prescribed Lan Gang train schedule, it will depart from Tianjin East Station at 9:30 PM and arrive at Pukou at 9:40 AM on Wednesday. The up train will also depart from Pukou at 7:00 AM on Mondays and Thursdays according to the Lan Gang train schedule and arrive at Tianjin East Station at 7:30 AM on Wednesdays and Saturdays. It will depart from the East Station at 9:00 PM and arrive at Liaoning at 5:00 PM the next day. It has also been decided that from November 25th, the existing No. 201 and No. 202 Lan Gang trains on this road will continue to operate according to the current schedule, with three trains running in both directions each week. Train No. 201 will depart from Tianjin at 9:30 PM on Tuesdays and Thursdays, and train No. 202 will depart from Pukou at 7:00 PM on Tuesdays and Fridays. This is hereby announced.

Direct Sino-U.S. Telegraph Communication 123

Zhenru Radio Station

Starts on the First of Next Month

The radio stations built by the Ministry of Communications in Zhenru and Liuhe for direct telegraph communication with the United States are nearing completion. Colonel Nance, the General Manager of the Philippine Radio Company, arrived in Shanghai on Thursday and plans to participate in the ceremony. From now on, direct telegraph communication between Shanghai and San Francisco will be possible, and its speed and accuracy will be far superior to submarine cables.

Wang Yansong Reports on the Fourth Plenary Session and Industry and Commerce 125

At the Memorial Ceremony of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce held a memorial week for the Premier in the auditorium yesterday morning. More than 100 members of the entire staff and representatives from various industries attended. Executive Committee Member Lao Jingxiu presided over the ceremony. Then, Wang Yansong, a standing committee member of the chamber, reported on the relationship between the Fourth Plenary Session and industry and commerce. A record of his speech is as follows:

Representatives, the most important event this week is of course the complete success of the Fourth Plenary Session. I think the success of the Fourth Plenary Session is not only an important event this week or even this year, but it occupies an extremely important page in the history of the success of the Chinese revolution, because this is a new era of construction that began after the elimination of the remaining warlords. There have been concrete resolutions and specific regulations in terms of party affairs, politics, and economy, and extremely serious corrections have been made to previous errors. I think that the spirit of great justice and sincerity of the Central Committee members can really arouse the unanimous admiration and support of the people of the whole country. With this sincere spirit, after the closing of the Plenary Session, all the resolutions will surely be implemented step by step. It will not be like the problem of "meeting but not passing, passing but not acting, and acting but not getting through" that President Hu said in his opening speech at the Fourth Plenary Session. The Fourth Plenary Session also had a very important and very close resolution on commerce, which is to revitalize industry and implement the abolition of likin from January 1, 1931. I think we have heard a lot of the voice of cutting likin in the Chamber of Commerce, and we are very annoyed by it. After the establishment of the National Government, it also convened meetings to discuss methods, issued orders, and stipulated dates, but in fact it was not able to effectively do it. Although the consumption tax to compensate for likin has been implemented for a long time, likin is still being collected there. We want to ask why the government cannot do the cutting of likin. The first major obstacle is really the division of the remaining warlords. On the one hand, these warlords expanded their private territories, recruited soldiers, and added generals to buy guns and cannons, but these guns, cannons, soldiers, and generals could not do without money. Therefore, the financial unification of the central government could not be carried out. In the several provinces they divided, they still had to collect likin, or even collect particularly heavy taxes. In this way, naturally, the cutting of likin suffered a great obstacle. No wonder the central government, even if it had resolutions, could not carry them out. Now, the warlords have been completely eliminated, and true unification has been realized. From now on, the central government's decrees can reach the whole country, and of course, the financial unification will not be a problem. The National Government, in accordance with the resolution of the Fourth Plenary Session, issued an order to abolish likin on January 1, 1931. May I ask which province would dare to resist? The decades of abuses suffered by our merchants will be lifted once and for all, and the development of industry and commerce will be inevitable. This is an extremely gratifying event. There is also a matter that is very closely related to merchants, and not only merchants, which is the strict suppression of bandits. The suffering of merchants from the Communist bandits in the past year or two is really hard to describe in words. To take a closer look, for example, the pig transportation industry in Jiangbei has suffered from the devastation of the Communist bandits in Taiyu. Kidnapping people and robbing goods is regarded as commonplace. If this continues, not only will the freight transportation not be smooth, but also the merchants will be hesitant to invest. Now, the Fourth Plenary Session has decided to strictly suppress the bandits, and Chairman Jiang will also inspect the three provinces of Xiang, Jiangxi, and Hubei, where the Communist bandits have wreaked the most havoc. As for the location of the capital and the neighboring provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, they will naturally pay close attention. It can be expected that the bandits will be suppressed in the near future. From now on, the Communist bandits can be suppressed, and likin will be abolished. I think the commercial sector will definitely be able to achieve the goal of "goods flowing smoothly." The other four major points of regularly convening national conferences, concentrating talent, improving the system, and completing local autonomy are all the wishes of the people of the whole country. The Fourth Plenary Session had clear resolutions on all of these. In the past, all matters were affected by the division of the remaining warlords, and the central government was busy suppressing the rebellious military. Now that Yan and Feng have left, the foundation of the party and the country is becoming more and more stable. Since the Fourth Plenary Session has made these resolutions, the government should be responsible for abiding by them, and the people should also do their best to assist and pay attention to practical work. All oral work, such as slogans and banners, articles, and all meetings that do not contribute to practical results should be reduced one by one. If everyone develops their spirits and buries themselves in work and does it conscientiously and practically, I think the results will be very impressive in three or five years. The brother feels that the importance of the relationship between the Fourth Plenary Session and industry and commerce will be presented as a brief report. At the end, the staff gave a lecture on the meaning of the party "titled Gandhi's non-cooperation doctrine."

Population Statistics Report for the City in September 127

The Municipal Public Security Bureau reports on population changes in the city every month. The August statistics were reported earlier. It is learned that the bureau's report for September shows that the number of households in each district of the city is 186,306 for regular households and 174,728 for attached households. The population is 972,985 for males and 719,350 for females. The number of foreign households is 2,014, and the population is 9,795. The total number of statistical households is 363,048, and the population is 1,702,130. The total population in the special district remains the same as the old statistics: 1,232,164 Chinese and 42,869 foreigners, adding up to a total population of 2,977,163 in the city, an increase of 13,030 in population compared to August.

Chinese Silk Disappears from the Korean Market 128

The Japanese government implements harsh taxes to curb the sales of Chinese silk

Merchants retreat, and Chinese silk has disappeared for six years

Chinese silk is particularly beautiful, inexpensive, and welcomed by Koreans

If harsh taxes are abolished through negotiations, sales will surely be prosperous again

The China National Products Maintenance Association specially entrusted Consul General Zhang Weicheng to conduct an on-the-ground investigation of the tax rate on Chinese silk in Korea in order to clarify the situation. Zhang Jun's reply to the association has been notified to the silk weaving industry groups in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces for reference. The original letter is recorded below:

Respectfully informing you that the Chinese Consulate General in Korea recently replied to a letter stating that it was entrusted to investigate the tax rate of Chinese silk in Korea and the preferences of the Korean people. After instructing the Chinese Chambers of Commerce in Pyongyang and Zhennampo to investigate, they replied. It is now being forwarded for your information. I hope that your organization will inform your members for reference.

Letter from the Chinese Consulate General in Korea, Business No. 83: I, the Consul General, have learned that the leaders of your branches and the Suzhou Cloud Brocade Guild inquired about the tax rate and sales of Chinese silk in Korea when passing through Shanghai. While this was being processed, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce ordered an investigation into the population tax levied by the resident country on our country's silk and silk fabrics, the previous tax rate, the current tax rate, the preferences of the people of that country for silk fabrics, and the sales of our country's silk fabrics in that place. We were asked to investigate and report in detail which item is the most sold. Upon receiving this order, we conducted separate investigations. We have now received reports from the Chinese Chambers of Commerce in Pyongyang and Zhennampo. In addition to reporting, we are extracting the relevant documents from the letters of each association for your reference. This is addressed to the China National Products Maintenance Association. Zhang Weicheng, Consul General of China in Korea, November 14, 1920, Republic of China.

Excerpt from the letter from the Pyongyang Chinese Chamber of Commerce (above omitted): Since the Japanese government implemented a tax rate of 100% on the value of our country's silk fabrics in 1924 in order to curb the sales of our country's silk fabrics, merchants have been troubled by the impact of this luxury tax rate. They are afraid of buying silk fabrics from their home country, just like tigers and wolves. Time flies, and our country's silk fabrics have disappeared from Pyongyang. It has been six years in the blink of an eye. Currently, only one or two companies sell summer cloth from Shanghai in the summer, but the sales volume is very small, not as prosperous as before the luxury tax rate. As for the preferences of Koreans in Pyongyang for our country's silk fabrics, it is enough to make our country's merchants hold great hope. Because our country's silk fabrics have exquisite patterns, solid quality, and durability, which cannot be compared with silk fabrics from other countries. No matter what kind of silk fabric from our country, it is welcomed and used by Koreans and praised for its good quality and low price. In short, the disappearance of our country's silk fabrics from the market for six years is all due to the luxury tax rate. If the government earnestly negotiates with the Japanese government with the spirit of national diplomacy to eliminate the luxury tax rate, how difficult would it be to restore the prosperous sales of silk fabrics as before? I hope that it will be forwarded for your reference. Zhennampo Chinese Chamber of Commerce's case, Letter No. 252 from your consulate, ordered us to investigate and report the population tax rate, people's preferences, and the majority of sales items of our country's silk fabrics and satin in the resident country. Upon receiving this order, our association has successively completed the investigation of this port and submitted the investigation table together with the document for your review and transmission.
