Establishment of the Yutang River Trade Union 129

First Committee Meeting Held Yesterday

The Yutang River Dredging Committee has been organized and established. The first committee meeting was held at 2:00 PM yesterday. Peng Yinqiao (represented by Peng Weiren), Wang Yiren, Yang Shunfan, Sun Shiben, Yang Fulin, and Ni Binzhi attended. Wu Wenhua and Cao Furu were present as observers. Wang Yiren presided over the meeting. Matters for discussion (1) How should the committee members for the top dredging and coordinated dredging be nominated? It was resolved that the notification should be based on the eighth district chief meeting, and the district offices should be notified to elect members as soon as possible for reporting. (2) Should a temporary director be nominated to take responsibility before the county bureau hires the director and deputy director? It was resolved to nominate Wang Yiren as the temporary director. (3) How should the dispute between the 14th and 16th districts be mediated? It was resolved to determine the following principles: (A) The 16th district will be temporarily exempt from levying this time. (B) The expenses that should be levied by the 16th district should be compensated by the 14th district increasing the number of earthworks by half in order to offset the loan. (C) In the future, the 16th district will cancel the Yutang dredging case of June 7th, Republic of China, and the 14th district will also cooperate in dredging the Liulei Pond. The above principles should be notified by the association to the third district office for separate notification, and a report should be submitted to the county government for record. (4) Discuss the date of the 10th meeting. It was resolved to set it on the 28th of this month.

Rally to Support Xiao and Oppose the Dutch 136

Scheduled to Open Tomorrow Afternoon

Please Have the Authorities Send Personnel to Guide

The rally to support Xiao and oppose the Dutch, organized by the Overseas Chinese Federation, Overseas Chinese Affairs Advancement Association, and 20 other groups in this city, is scheduled to be held tomorrow at the City Chamber of Commerce. Yesterday, the association specially submitted a document to the Longhua Garrison Headquarters, the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, requesting that they send personnel to attend and provide guidance. The original document and response letters from various parties are compiled as follows:

Document to the Three Agencies: Respectfully, the news that Ms. Xiao Xin'an, a female teacher from our country, was brutally raped by the first and second mates of the Jabaad, a steamer of the Java Company, in a planned and organized manner, has aroused universal indignation. In addition, the Dutch government has massacred tens of thousands of our overseas Chinese compatriots over the years, and imprisoned and expelled countless party committee reporters and teachers. In its governing Dutch constitution, it openly stipulates that Chinese people are an inferior race, in the same category as indigenous people, which is even more intolerable. Therefore, we are jointly initiating and scheduling the Shanghai All-Circles Rally to Support Xiao and Oppose the Dutch on November 26th (Wednesday) at 1 p.m. at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce at Tianhou Bridge to discuss various measures to assist Ms. Xiao and alleviate the suffering of overseas Chinese compatriots in the Dutch colonies. This matter concerns the patriotic movement, and we earnestly request your honorable leadership to approve sending personnel to attend and provide guidance, so as to avoid mistakes. We are extremely grateful.

Ningbo Fellow-Villagers Association Letter: Respectfully, we previously received your letter from the 12th of November, regarding the insult suffered by Ms. Xiao Xin'an when she went abroad. You requested that we join the support association to discuss methods of avenging her and alleviating the suffering of overseas Chinese compatriots in the Dutch colonies. Upon receiving this, we replied and submitted it to the 16th executive committee meeting of our association. Everyone agreed that Ms. Xiao, a priest traveling to the South Seas, suffered a strange humiliation, which is extremely infuriating. It was unanimously resolved to join and follow your association to jointly plan resistance, etc. Accordingly, we are sending this letter for your information. Respectfully, Overseas Chinese Federation.

Warning to Lin Guogeng: Overseas Chinese Expelled from the Capital Are Extremely Angry at the Xiamen Garrison Commander's Interference in the Xiao Case, and Specifically Sent a Telegram to Advise Lin Guogeng Not to Be a Running Dog of Imperialism. The telegram said: Commander Lin of Xiamen, be advised that since the Xiao case occurred, the whole country has been indignant. Please do not interfere with the boycott of Dutch goods movement. If you violate public opinion and willingly act as a running dog of imperialism, this association vows to deal with you to the death. Overseas Chinese Expelled from British and Dutch Colonies in Southeast Asia Support Association for Promoting National Diplomacy.

Please Prevent Leasing the Wharf: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company recently has a plan to lease the China Merchants Wharf to the Java Company. The Fifth Wharf Workers' Union of the company believes that the Xiao case has not yet been resolved, and it seems inappropriate for the company to suddenly lease the wharf to the Java Company that caused the Xiao case. Therefore, they sent a letter to the Xiao Case Support Association yesterday requesting negotiations with the company to prevent this. The original letter is recorded below: Respectfully, we have recently learned that our company's China Merchants Wharf will be leased to the Dutch merchant Java Company. Now that your support association is leading the anti-Dutch movement, please pay attention to this. We earnestly request that you send a letter to the General Management Office of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to seriously prevent this before the Xiao case is resolved. Respectfully, Xiao Case Support Association.

Small Kidnapping Case on Pingliang Road 137

Taking Advantage of the Situation to Kidnap a Child

Demanding a Ransom of a Thousand Dollars

Five robbers, speaking with a Jiangbei accent, broke into the home of Long Yuankui at No. 487 Pingliang Road, Yangshupu, at about 11 a.m. yesterday. They intimidated the victim with guns and arbitrarily searched the premises for half an hour before leaving. The exact amount of clothing and cash stolen is unknown. The robbers were not satisfied with what they got and kidnapped his two-year-old child named Shu Xin, claiming that they would only release him for a ransom of a thousand dollars.

Self-Confessed Kidnapper 138

Sent to Court for Trial

Ji Zhengxing, a Yancheng native residing near Yangjing, Pudong, reported to the Second Branch of the Third District a week ago that his daughter, San Guniang, was kidnapped by Zhou Guangwen, Zhou Guangcheng, Zhou Guangwu, Zhou Guangsheng, and Zhou Wu, five brothers, who demanded a ransom. He requested that they be arrested and investigated. The police immediately arrested Zhou Guangcheng and Zhou Guangwu, while the rest fled. The police believed that the case involved accusing kidnappers, so they transferred the arrested persons to the District Court for investigation. Meanwhile, they notified Lu Changgao, Zhou's second landlord, to hand over Zhou Guangwen within a week for verification. Yesterday, Zhou Guangwen suddenly surrendered to the police station with Qiu Changwen, claiming that Ji Zhengxing was his uncle-in-law. The kidnapping of his daughter, San Guniang, on the 7th of this month, as alleged in the case, was completely false. His daughter had gone to the home of relatives in the South Wharf. He was falsely accused of kidnapping and his brother was arrested. He panicked and fled to Puxi. Now he has come to the police station to surrender. Regardless of whether it is true or not, he should be handed over immediately. He was immediately presented to the Public Security Bureau and transferred to the court for trial.

Distributing Regulations on Joint Police-Civilian Defense 139

Yuan Liang, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, drafted regulations on joint police-civilian defense for winter defense matters, printed them into easy-to-understand explanations of bandit prevention rules, and distributed them to the directors of various districts and stations under his jurisdiction, who immediately dispatched police to distribute them to all households and businesses in the city to prevent bandits from robbing during the cold winter months. Municipal Public Works Bureau Rectifies Private Alley Street Lights 140

Investigate...Tenants Must Report Clearly

Rectify...Property Owners Must Install Quickly

The Municipal Public Works Bureau is actively rectifying street lights in the city, sparing no effort. All highway street lights have been replaced and added with new styles as much as possible, and the lights are neat, bright and radiant, changing the previous dilapidated and dim appearance, which is very beneficial to traffic and security. As for private alley street lights, the bureau believes that their nature should be managed by the property owners themselves. Therefore, since June of the 18th year, all private alley street lights in the city have been the responsibility of the property owners. However, it has been found that there are places in various neighborhoods that have no street lights, or that have no street lights and the installations are unsuitable or poorly managed. Therefore, in early April of the 19th year, the Municipal Government approved and promulgated the Regulations on Eliminating Private Street Lights to rectify this situation. To facilitate the property owners, measures were formulated for the bureau to install private street lights on their behalf, stipulating that property owners could request the bureau to install or manage them on their behalf, as long as they bear the corresponding costs of labor and materials or management. The bureau's handling of this work starts with an investigation. First, the Public Security Bureau's various district stations are asked to report private alleys without street lights, and then the bureau sends personnel to conduct on-site investigations to facilitate gradual rectification. However, there are quite a few tenants who do not know the situation and are hesitant to answer directly when investigators inquire about the names and addresses of property owners, making it impossible to understand. On the property owner's side, they often delay installation or improvement, which is a lack of cooperation. Private alley street lights are large enough to prevent the concealment of petty thieves and facilitate the arrest of police officers, which is related to public security. Small lights do not cause the hardship of groping and bumping around at night, which is beneficial to the residents. In the property owner's layout of this bright and convenient facility, it can also make the property rental popular and increase its value. Therefore, private alley street lights are not only required by the municipal government to strictly rectify, but also property owners and tenants should work together to make them universally installed and always keep them bright.

Municipal Workers' Union Declaration on the Xin Case 141

Important Meeting of All Circles Xin Case Support Association Today

Since the Sampan Man Xin Dingxiang was pushed into the Huangpu River by French sailors for no reason and died tragically by drowning, all circles in Shanghai have been deeply indignant and have organized support associations to achieve the goals of punishing the murderers and compensating for the losses. The municipal government has also repeatedly negotiated with the French authorities through Secretary Geng Jiaji. Although there have been expressions of punishing the murderers and compensating for the losses, there are no definite measures. Therefore, the Xin Case Support Association of all circles is still actively proceeding and has scheduled another important meeting at the Ningbo Fellow-Villagers Association at 2 p.m. today. Yesterday, all workers' unions in the city also jointly issued a declaration to support the Xin case. The full text is recorded below:

To the National Compatriots: Since the tragic case of Xin Dingxiang being pushed into the Huangpu River and drowned by French sailors occurred, the Shanghai labor unions, seeing that their compatriots were innocently killed by foreigners, for the sake of the country's status and the protection of the nation, were outraged and organized support associations to proceed separately. On the one hand, in the name of all Shanghai labor unions, they requested the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to inform the French imperialists to punish the chief culprits and to pursue compensation and pensions. On the other hand, they engaged in various propaganda activities to awaken the Chinese nation to resist the French imperialists and to demand that the whole country sympathize with and assist in the tragic death of Xin Dingxiang. Although we have been calling out until our lips are parched and our strength is exhausted, we are still continuing unremittingly, which is enough to express the spirit of the national movement that has been madly developed. Considering that this has happened, although the government has negotiated and the labor unions have assisted one after another, the French imperialists are cunning and sly, and they have submerged the facts and sold hypocrisy to deceive people in an attempt to deal with the matter with compromise. Alas, national compatriots, are we human beings or are we different from foreign people? The imperialists openly picked up and killed foreign compatriots in the 20th century civilized country, killing them in a way that was worse than being a slave. Is this right? Therefore, we believe that any imperialist's ambitious and arbitrary killing of our compatriots is to reduce the country's strength and to eliminate our country. Therefore, the massacre of our compatriots is the consistent policy of the imperialists to love the country and preserve the nation. We earnestly hope that the national compatriots will unite and rise up in response to the tragic death of Xin Dingxiang by French sailors and become a powerful backing for the government. We will not rest until we achieve the goals of punishing the murderers, compensating for the losses, apologizing, and guaranteeing that similar incidents will not occur in the future. We hereby declare this.

A Scene of Deception 142

Liang Jintang Cleverly Uses a Beauty Trap

Xu Qichang Loses Over a Hundred Dollars

Meeting on the Road, Accusing Each Other in Court

Liang Huangzhen Marries an Indian Again

Xu Qichang, a Shaoxing native residing at No. 1036 Wuzhou Road, Hongkou, is forty-five years old and saddened by the loss of his wife. His Cantonese friend Liang Jintang knew that he wanted to remarry and wanted to take the opportunity to defraud him. He came up with a plan. On June 12th of this year, he specially went to Xu's residence and said that he had lost his job in Shanghai and urgently wanted to return to his hometown, but he had no boat to Guangzhou. If he wanted to stay, he had no place to live. Xu thought of their friendship, so he housed and fed him. After Liang lived there for several days, he suddenly went out and brought back two young women. He introduced them to Xu, saying that one named Liang Huizhen was Liang's elder sister, and one named Liang Huifang was Liang's younger sister, both of whom were not yet married. The two felt affection for each other and planned to have the elder sister offer herself as a wife. Xu was just about to do so, so he allowed the three siblings to live in his residence. Liang also said that after he returned to Guangzhou to inform his mother, he would come to Shanghai again to proceed with the elder sister's marriage. Then he borrowed thirty gold dollars from Xu as travel expenses to return to his hometown. On the morning of the 14th of this month, Liang said that there was a boat going to Guangzhou and he had to go to a certain steamship wharf to buy a ticket first. At this time, Xu and Liang had changed from friends to prospective family, so he saw Liang off at the steamship wharf with a heartfelt farewell. After Xu returned home, he delayed until noon before returning. Then the sister flowers were gone. He checked the suitcases and all the leather and silk clothes were gone. The estimated loss was about one hundred and seventy dollars. Xu then realized that he had met a con artist. Because he had no way to find out where those people were, he left it alone. Until the afternoon of the other day, Xu was strolling on Zhoujiazui Road and unexpectedly met Liang Huizhen. He immediately arrested her and took her to the Harbin Police Station. She confessed that Liang Jintang and Liang Huifang were hiding at No. 1907 Dongyouheng Road. They were taken to that place and arrested together. Under investigation, it was said that Liang Huizhen had married an Indian named Ara Mayut on the 12th of this month as his wife. However, when the detective sent a Western detective to the British Consulate to inquire, the British Consulate did not issue the marriage certificate for the two. Yesterday morning, they were all sent to the Special District Court, where Judge Feng Shide questioned them. Xu Qichang detailed the experience of being cheated. The defendant Liang Jintang confessed that Liang was having an affair with my elder sister Huizhen and I did not introduce them. My sister Huifang and I lived in Xu's house and were also invited by Xu. That day I went to the steamship wharf to find a boat and Xu did not go with me. My sister took her clothes and bag with her and went to the French Concession with my sister because my sister said that she did not need to return to Xu's house, so she stayed in a hotel for a few days and then we separated. Liang Huifang also confessed that Xu had an affair with my sister and then ordered my siblings to live in his house. Later, my sister pawned her clothes. Liang Huizhen confessed that in May I met Xu on the road and he immediately used seduction to take me to a hotel and sleep with me for one night. Then Xu said that he was very rich, so I married him. I did take the clothes and they were taken after I separated from Xu. On the 12th of this month, I officially married an Indian in the church. The Indian Ara Mayut also came to court and translated that he had married Huizhen at the Muslim Church at No. 1 Zhejiang Road on the 12th of this month. The officiant was a Chinese pastor. Although the British Consulate has not issued the marriage certificate, it will issue it together with the passport after the British Consulate verifies it when it returns home. Judge Feng ordered that the three defendants, Liang Jintang, etc., be detained separately for further investigation because the police station still needed to investigate.

Ling Baoyuan's Sand Boat Robbed in Lishun Port 145

The sand boat Ling Baoyuan recently loaded 4,000 dan of yellow sprouts in Jiaozhou, Shandong, and sailed to Shanghai to hand them over to a certain receiving agency. On the 19th of this month, when it sailed on the sea surface of Lishun Port, more than 100 li outside Wusongkou, it suddenly encountered two pirate ships sailing towards it, firing guns at the Ling boat and ordering it to stop. The Ling boat saw this and pulled up the sails and sped forward, but was spotted by the pirates who fired their guns and sailed after it. The Ling boat was hit by many bullets and three crew members were also wounded by the bullets. All the crew members were panicked and the two pirate ships chased after it. The pirates swarmed onto the ship with guns and searched everywhere. They did not see any silver dollars, which angered the pirates, who beat the crew members and searched them for everything they had. They forced the Ling boat to sail and the two pirate ships guarded behind it. They sailed to the coast of Jiangbei and stopped. The pirates searched again and beat the shipowner, forcing him to hand over the silver dollars. The shipowner replied that there were no silver dollars in the ship. The pirates moved his bedding boxes, etc., to the pirate ship. The pirates left the ship and took five crew members away, telling the shipowner to prepare the money and come to redeem them quickly. The two pirate ships fled to the sea area of Jiangbei. After the pirates left, the Ling boat sailed to the Zhihe River and stopped. The injured crew members were sent to the hospital. Yesterday, the shipowner took a train to Shanghai to report the various cargo numbers and hired a boat to unload the cargo in the ship. Only the Ling boat had to be repaired before it could sail. The loss has already been considerable.

The Judge Ordered the Family of the Deceased to Sue in Court

The Western police chief replied that the police station did not deliberately refuse to file a lawsuit because detectives were sent to the scene of the accident immediately after the incident to investigate. However, the shop assistants in the nearby shops all claimed that they did not pay attention to the situation at the time, so the police station could not obtain evidence and failed to prosecute. Xu then ordered Jiang Shuangquan to sign a guarantee to receive the body for coffining and burial and ordered him to file a lawsuit in court.

Shi Jingen's Lumber Swindle Exposed 156

Once is bad enough; must it happen again?

Fengtai Lumber Company at the New Wharf in the southern part of the city has been open for quite some time and usually has prosperous business. A few days ago, a man resembling a worker came to the company and claimed that he was sent by the owner of Xu Yuanji Construction Company at No. 12 Chezhan Road to purchase lumber and other materials. After speaking, he presented a slip of paper from the construction company, which was stamped with the company's letterhead seal. Since the lumber company had previous dealings with Xu Yuanji and saw the stamped note, they did not suspect anything. The staff member came out to serve him and, as usual, the man selected many top-grade timbers and hired a cart to transport them away. Afterwards, the lumber company sent a staff member to Xu Yuanji to collect the receipt, but the construction company said that they had not sent anyone to pick up the goods, nor had they issued a note as proof. The staff member reported back to the company, and they realized that they had been swindled, but the goods had already been taken away and there was nothing they could do but sigh in vain. Unexpectedly, yesterday at around 9 a.m., the man came to the company again, wanting to select and purchase lumber. The company immediately asked him to wait a moment while notifying Xu Yuanji to send a staff member, Zhou Yongsheng, from Pudong, to come and investigate. He found that there was no such person in the factory and realized that he was a swindler. He immediately went outside and summoned the police officer Zhang Yingxu, who was on duty at the 13th guard post in the area. They arrested the man and took him to the First Precinct of the First Division. During the preliminary trial by the station chief, the man confessed that his name was Shi Jingen, 19 years old, from Pudong, and that he lived on Fumin Road and worked as a carpenter. He knew that Xu Yuanji had dealings with the lumber company, so he privately carved the company's seal and impersonated them to take the lumber from the lumber company. He had been quite successful the first time, so he planned to try this trick again, but unexpectedly he was arrested. Because the matter involved a fraud case, he was ordered to prepare a document to be sent to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

An Appeal from the Jiangxi Disaster Relief Association 159

The Jiangxi Disaster Relief Association submitted a document to Chairman Jiang, which stated: "Submitting this document on behalf of the gentlemen and merchants who have suffered in eastern Jiangxi, who have come to appeal and present their views to Your Excellency. Since last winter, the bandit forces in the counties under the jurisdiction of Guangxin Prefecture in eastern Jiangxi have been rampant, and land and water transportation to and from Nanchang has been cut off. As a result, refugees from the six counties above Yiyang and Hengfeng have been taking the counties under the jurisdiction of Quzhou, Zhejiang, as their temporary homes for more than ten months. The elderly and young are helping each other, like ants, and the total number is unknown, perhaps millions, and their situation is extremely miserable. Recently, we heard that Your Excellency's suppression of the rebels has been successful, the great difficulties have been overcome, and the triumphant song has echoed far and wide. Everyone believes that the government has ample time and the military has ample strength, and that the small rebels in the remote corners are not worth defeating. Therefore, representatives from all walks of life have been gathered and sent to the capital to present four suggestions for restoring security in eastern Jiangxi. When Your Excellency passed through Shanghai, we personally presented the original text. I believe that you will consider the fact that this association is a relief organization. They have come to appeal and express their feelings with tears in their eyes, requesting another word to be heard. The plea is sincere, and we dare not refuse. We have carefully examined the opinions expressed by the refugees: (1) Please send a brigade of troops to enter eastern Jiangxi from Zhejiang. (2) Please issue a clear order to specially appoint Guo Tong, a gentleman from Shangrao, to return to his hometown to handle post-disaster relief and local cleansing matters. (3) Please issue a clear order to allocate salt tax revenues from eastern Jiangxi for post-disaster expenses. (4) Please lend one or two million in public bonds to provide disaster relief. After researching these suggestions, the members of this association believe that they are reasonable and feasible. We respectfully present a detailed explanation to Your Excellency. Your Excellency’s newly transferred divisions are entering Jiangxi from Jiujiang, heading to Nanchang and Raozhou to separately suppress the two groups of bandits in western and eastern Jiangxi. The bandit forces in western Jiangxi are extremely strong and close to Nanchang, so it is natural to enter from Jiujiang. For the moment, we will not discuss this. Although the bandit forces in eastern Jiangxi are not very strong, their nests are actually within the territory of Guangxin, relying on the mountains for support. The only way to pursue them is by going upstream from Raozhou, which is only about 400 miles by boat and takes half a month. Moreover, the northeastern border of Guangxin relies on the Xianxia, Jin, and Da Mountains for its dangerous terrain. If the army chases from below, it will inevitably force the bandits to flee into the mountains and escape to the borders of Zhejiang, Anhui, and Fujian. If we want to completely eliminate them, it will inevitably take time. The difficulties of Tonggu in the early Qing Dynasty and the occupation of Guangzhou and Yuanzhou by Hong Yang required several years of effort to overcome. The lessons of the past should be heeded. Moreover, today, the borders of Zhejiang and Anhui are where refugees from eastern Jiangxi are secretly resting. If the bandits are forced to flee there, will it not be like hungry tigers entering a flock of sheep? If heavy troops advance along two routes, with one brigade entering from Raozhou to quell the chaos and another brigade entering Yushan from Quzhou to adopt a containment strategy, making it impossible for the bandits to flee into the mountains, then they can be eliminated in the shortest possible time. The advantages are: First, troops can reach Yanzhou from Hangzhou by waterway and then walk to Yushan in four days, which is less than one-third of the time it takes from Raozhou. Second, refugees along the Zhejiang border can gradually return to their hometowns as the troops advance, avoiding the increasing cold in winter and the fear of bandits fleeing. Third, it is more difficult to suppress the bandits if they enter the mountains. Raozhou and the area below are mostly plains and swamps. The bandits are skilled at using mountains, but they lack the cover of plains, the artillery for hiding in swamps, and the boats for crossing water. Therefore, if they are forced from above to flee below, the roots can be completely eradicated. Fourth, it is necessary to divide the troops and enter from Zhejiang. The bandits have occupied eastern Jiangxi for years and implemented a land distribution system, so all the people who have not fled have been assimilated by the bandits, which is why the bandits are not easy to suppress because the people are helping them. If we kill all of them at this time, it would be a terrible tragedy. If we ignore them, it will be easy for them to be used by the bandits. Therefore, local cleansing is necessary when the army arrives. The fields have been flattened by the bandits, and all the deeds and maps have been looted. The displaced people have long suffered from hunger and cold and are eager to return home to rebuild their livelihoods. If they are prevented from returning, they will have no food or clothing. If they are allowed to return on their own, they will ultimately have no way to make a living. If the fields are not cleared, there will be no way to cultivate them. If the people do not cultivate them, there will ultimately be no food or clothing. Therefore, post-disaster relief is necessary. All of these measures require local, fair-minded gentry to take responsibility. Guo Tong, a standing director of this association, is from Shangrao County. He is an honest, upright, experienced, and knowledgeable person. The people of eastern Jiangxi praise him. He has duties at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, but his hometown has urged him to uphold justice. His family's home, family, and property have been severely damaged, so he is filled with righteous indignation and is willing to restore security in eastern Jiangxi as his own responsibility. If Your Excellency could personally appoint him as a special envoy for post-disaster relief and allow him to take a few months of leave to return with the army to handle all post-disaster affairs, he would be able to work with the fair-minded gentry and merchants in various places to properly plan everything. Establishing a foundation of good governance in eastern Jiangxi based on the principle of self-governance would be helpful to other places. Moreover, we have heard that a secretary recently dispatched by the province has been given full authority to gather the security regiments of Shangrao, Yushan, and Guangfeng counties, obtaining hundreds of guns and mobilizing tens of thousands of refugees to cleanse the countryside. From Shangrao downwards, they have gradually reached the border of Hengfeng County. The regiment soldiers have no training and are using the name of suppressing bandits to buy and sell refugees. They are mostly motivated by revenge and are indiscriminate in their killing, targeting anyone they see as a threat. This will result in eastern Jiangxi suffering another great calamity. The social order in eastern Jiangxi has been completely destroyed. At this time, land taxes cannot be collected, public assets have been wiped out, and it is impossible to collect donations from the private property of the people. If we want to seek post-disaster relief, wouldn't it be the same as trying to cook without rice if we don't separately allocate a large sum of money? The request to allocate revenues from the Yushan tax and donation bureaus for temporary use in local areas is a fair solution. However, the salt import donation from Zhejiang in Yushan, when it was well-governed, amounted to 60,000 units per year, with each unit being three dan and each dan being donated 6 jiao of silver, which has recently increased to 2.4 yuan, totaling about 40,000 yuan per year. This is an additional harsh tax outside the law. The people's strength has been exhausted after the chaos, and in theory, it should be exempt. Moreover, since the bandit rebellion, the population has sharply declined, and the sales have been less than 20-30%. At this time, rather than allowing it to be embezzled, it is better to clearly allocate it for public use in the local area. This is also a reasonable approach. However, it must be clearly stated that the donation amount should not be increased again due to the decrease in sales. This is necessary in view of the increasing trend in the past. The special consumption tax in Yushan is about 100,000 yuan per year, but it has also sharply declined. Those who are embezzling have long been silent and have not paid a penny for the bandit rebellion, so it is okay to allocate it for post-disaster relief. However, the total monthly revenue of the two bureaus is only 30,000 yuan. At this time, the first thing to do for post-disaster relief is to rectify the soldiers and police. The monthly salaries have always been in arrears, allowing them to exploit the local people. Only after everything is done well for the post-disaster relief, then the small sum of tens of thousands of yuan is far from enough. After repeated research, the members of this association believe that, during the period of bandit suppression and local cleansing in eastern Jiangxi, all tax revenues in various places should be designated for use. For example, Yushan and Guangfeng counties have suffered less damage, and Qianshan also has 10-20% of its security remaining. It is only because transportation to and from Nanchang has been cut off that it has been impossible to investigate and transfer the full amount for embezzlement. At this time, the full amount should be allocated for use, so that everything can be heard and supported. Those who collect and use the money must not embezzle it. The various post-disaster affairs can be carried out quickly. In no more than two or three months, security will gradually return to its former state. By then, all revenue will belong to the provincial treasury. The people of the fifteen counties in eastern Jiangxi used to number over six million. The most severely affected by this disaster are Yiyang, Hengfeng, and Shangrao in Guangxin, and Dexing, Poyang, and Fuliang in Raozhou. The total number of refugees in Zhejiang and Anhui is no less than two million. When they return to their hometowns, even if a few houses have survived, their homes are like being washed by water. Utensils, farm tools, and seeds are all gone. How can they resume their businesses and wait for a good harvest? Therefore, it is absolutely necessary to distribute disaster relief funds. The request to borrow public bonds is also very good. The country should be generous when it is in a time of hardship and should be happy to distribute wealth and grains. This is the good model for ancient kings to bring stability and governance, which Your Excellency should adopt. We propose that the National Disaster Relief Committee be ordered to properly plan the method of borrowing, so that the issuance of national bonds will actually ease the suffering of the people, and the repayment of the funds in the future will avoid burdening the national treasury. The cost-free approach is actually the good policy of today. However, the history of governance in Jiangxi is stained with corruption. Last year, the disaster relief funds issued by the central government to Shangrao and Hengfeng counties under the jurisdiction of Guangxin were embezzled by the county magistrates and never reached the people. Therefore, the refugees have separately submitted a report to Your Excellency for investigation. Although this matter is small, its impact is great. If the grace is not extended to the people, then all the good policies planned by the central government will be empty talk. We hope that Your Excellency will take charge and reverse this trend. The views of the members of this association are largely the same as those of the refugees. We dare not be biased towards them because of our hometown ties. To govern well, one must be impartial and consider both internal and external affairs. This is a consistent principle from ancient times to the present, both in China and abroad. Your Excellency's declaration of suppressing bandits and governing with justice and the issuance of announcements have been met with joy throughout the country. Now, what the refugees are saying is nothing more than to promote Your Excellency's intentions so that they can be put into practice. The sympathy of the assembly for the refugees is not only helpful to Your Excellency. Although the matter belongs to a corner of eastern Jiangxi, the reputation established is enough to encourage the loyalty of the twenty-seven provinces. The matter is of great importance. We hope that Your Excellency will embrace the spirit of caring for those who are drowning and feeding those who are hungry. The world has been yearning for good governance for a long time. Therefore, this association dares to plead on behalf of the millions of fathers, elders, and brothers in our hometown. We ask that you accept the feelings of the people and promptly adopt and implement them. The foundation for a peaceful and prosperous world may well begin in eastern Jiangxi. Anxious to express our words, we respectfully submit this document to the Chairman of the National Government, Jiang."

Large Seizure of Heroin Leads to Investigation and Thorough Examination of Smugglers 161

Six of the Seized Boxes Were Shipped by Ming Song Foreign Firm

Shipping Company Cables Europe to Inquire About Eastern Smuggling Organizations

The case of a large quantity of heroin being found on an Italian mail ship has been reported previously. Due to the request of the Anti-Drug Association, the customs tax commissioner is investigating the individuals who smuggled the drugs to clarify the truth and trace the source of smuggling. This matter is currently under thorough investigation. The various developments in this case are recorded as follows:

Customs Continues to Inspect Drugs: The customs inspected the drugs seized for the second time on the Italian ship "Cortellena," totaling 33 boxes. When the customs officers opened the boxes, they found a large quantity of heroin. Since the ship carried a large amount of cargo, it was possible that more drugs were mixed in with other items. In view of the fact that three boxes were missed during the first search and were taken away by smugglers, the Jianghai Customs dispatched officials to the Gonghexing warehouse to continue inspecting the cargo arriving in Shanghai on the ship. They discovered more than 30 boxes of suspicious goods, and after consulting with the shipping warehouse, they were moved to the customs and combined with the 33 boxes that had already been seized. At the same time, the goods were taken out and chemically tested. The testing has not yet been completed, but it is reported that a large amount of drugs has been found.

Non-Drugs Returned: Among the 60 boxes of goods seized by the Jianghai Customs, seven boxes of "Cleansing Material" raw materials for writing and washing materials have been tested and confirmed to be free of drugs. Yesterday, the customs sent them back to the Italian shipping company to notify the customers to pick them up. The other goods have not been returned because the testing procedures have not been completed. The shipping company has not sent anyone to sign for and pick them up, indicating that they are afraid to do so.

Japanese Trading Company Involved in Drug Trafficking: The three boxes that were missed during the first search and taken away, as well as the six boxes in the second search, were all signed for by the Japanese trading company "Mcisbo Co." During the second signing for the six boxes, the customs detained them and found that they were all heroin. It has now been confirmed that the Chinese name of the company is "Ming Song Foreign Firm," and that it is responsible for receiving the nine items in both searches. They do not admit responsibility for the rest.

Shipping Bureau Cables Italy to Inquire: After discovering this large quantity of drugs, the Jianghai Customs sent personnel to the Italian shipping company to thoroughly investigate the Shanghai handling company. The Italian company produced bills of lading that did not have any pre-filled signing company names, so there was no way to know the buyers. Recently, due to the inquiry from the Anti-Drug Association, the Italian shipping company also wants to understand the origin and whereabouts of the goods. Yesterday, it sent a telegram to the Fiester Triest head office to inquire about the "Transport Internationaux" company that declared the goods and to inquire about the names of the purchasing companies and cargo owners in Shanghai, Dalian, and Tianjin, requesting that they be investigated and sent to Shanghai as soon as possible to clarify the situation. Once the head office replies, the Eastern smuggling organization for this drug trafficking can be identified.

Cargo Inspected Item by Item: Since the incident occurred, the Jianghai Customs has issued a general order requiring that all goods shipped from Europe and the United States to Shanghai, which were previously sampled for inspection, must now be opened and inspected item by item by the inspectors, and no perfunctory work is allowed to prevent drugs from entering. Therefore, the inspection of European goods arriving in Shanghai recently has been very serious, and the procedures for picking up goods have become unusually cumbersome.

Business Gift Certificates Must Have Revenue Stamps 162

Because Their Nature is Similar to Goods Vouchers and Deposit Slips

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to various trade associations yesterday, stating: "We hereby inform you that we received a public letter No. 28 from the Jiangsu Revenue Stamp Bureau on the 22nd of this month. The letter stated that it was acting in compliance with the order of the Jiangsu Revenue Stamp Bureau, which stated that it was following the instructions of the Ministry of Finance's Seal No. 23703, which contained a petition from Wang Zhentang, stating that, in the interest of financial management, tax rectification should come first. He has found that various gift certificates issued by major stores in various commercial ports have not been affixed with revenue stamps. Now, various deeds, account books, and invoices are all affixed with revenue stamps separately, but only gift certificates, regardless of the item or value, are not affixed with revenue stamps. This seems very unfair compared to ordinary tickets and certificates that are affixed with revenue stamps. Stores collect cash when issuing the certificates, but the tax authorities do not investigate. If the gift certificates are not guaranteed, they will become worthless pieces of paper once the store goes bankrupt. He is requesting that the ministry discuss and develop methods to classify and affix revenue stamps according to value, so as to regulate them. This would make the issuance of gift certificates by stores more credible, facilitate the exchange of gifts in society, and contribute to national taxation. In response to this, it has been found that the gift certificates, if they refer to goods on the face of the certificate, are goods vouchers issued by shops according to the provisional regulations of the revenue stamp tax. If they refer to a sum of money, they are deposit slips, and revenue stamps should be affixed separately according to regulations. In addition to issuing and distributing the above, the bureau should order the sub-bureaus to immediately forward a letter to the Chamber of Commerce to notify the various shops to comply with the regulations and ask for a reply. We have approved this request and are hereby forwarding the letter to you. Please investigate and notify the shops under your jurisdiction to comply with the regulations."

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 171

— Sea Wanderer

Mother: Why are you clenching your teeth again because of a toothache?

Child (stroking his cheek, saying with a crying voice): Yes, Mom, this damned tooth really hurts terribly.

Mother: It's your own fault for being greedy and eating sweets.

Child: Mom, it's not related. When I eat sweets, all my teeth are biting together, but the only tooth that hurts today is just one.

A: You must be very pleased these days since you're newly married.

B: Pleased, of course, very pleased, but there's nothing to do.

A: Then how do you amuse yourselves?

B: The two of us sit facing each other all day long, just staring at each other. I envy her for marrying a good husband, and she envies me for marrying a good wife.

Host (awakened in the middle of the night by a sound): Who's there? What are you doing here?

Thief (answering in the dark): It's me. I'm here to find some money. Don't move, or I'll take your life.

Host: Let me get up and light a candle to help you find it. Maybe there are some lost copper coins in the corners of the floor.

A: I've suffered from wearing shoes my whole life; I'd rather go barefoot.

B: What's the matter?

A: Wearing new ones hurts my toes, and wearing old ones is embarrassing.

Research on the Lyrics of "Yutang Chun" 172

— Shaoqing

Xun Huisheng sings "Yutang Chun" (Gao Ting Company has this record, and Cheng Yanqiu also sings "Yutang Chun," Yuan Ban). The er-liu tune says, "Sending the gentleman back to his original prefecture, the two of them swore an oath before the lamp. The gentleman vowed not to marry another, and Yutang Chun vowed not to marry until death." Yanqiu's lyrics are different from this. Yanqiu's lyrics say, "Since the gentleman went to Nanjing, Yutang Chun is making up an illness in the north tower. If the gentleman does not marry me, Yutang Chun will keep her chastity and not marry." In one word, the difference is that one mentions swearing an oath under the lamp at night, and the other does not mention swearing an oath but only says that after the gentleman left, Yutang Chun feigned illness. The old lyrics say, "Sending the gentleman back to Nanjing, the two of them swore an oath before the gods," which means they swore an oath before the gods at the Guanyu Temple when they parted. The difference between the drama lyrics before the lamp and before the gods is like this.

Also, in the lyrics of Pi Huang, the "dong" rhyme and the "ren chen" rhyme are never used together, but the old lyrics of "Yutang Chun" have "Wang Jinlong," "to Hongtong," and "face flushing red," etc. The words "long," "tong," and "hong" are all in the "zhong dong" rhyme and cannot be used together. Now, Yanqiu's lyrics have changed "Wang Jinlong" to "three officials," and "face flushing red" to "face containing truth." Only the sentence "to Hongtong" has not been changed, and the word "tong" is still out of rhyme. It is difficult to think of a suitable way to change the sentence.

The old lyrics say, "Thirty-six thousand taels of silver turned to ashes in an instant." Some people say that thirty-six thousand taels of silver cannot be exhausted in "an instant," so Yanqiu changed it to "all." "Dan" and "gai" are both departing-tone words, which do not cause any change in the melody, so it doesn't matter.

The Sheng lyrics say, "The matchmaker's money is three hundred taels," while Yanqiu's lyrics say "one hundred taels." Whether it is three hundred taels or one hundred taels is a small problem. Looking at the previous singing, there is "three hundred taels of patterned silver at the first meeting," and in the white speech, there is also "there are more than three hundred taels in one hand." If there is another three hundred taels, it seems repetitive, so one hundred taels is more appropriate. These numbers are all written arbitrarily by the book writers and playwrights and are not facts, so it doesn't matter much. Three words need to be sung loudly, and one word is sung softly.

"First hit the gold cup and jade cup" is an old lyric, and it is still used by many people today. Gold cups can be hit, but jade cups cannot be hit, so the word "hit" should be changed to "buy."

"Then buy green plate and green bottle" is also a common lyric. Now Yanqiu changed it to "and buy green plate and vase." There is no big difference here.

"The procuress, greedy for money, sold me, sold me to Shen Yanling." This lyric by Yanqiu is very good. There is no explicit mention of selling to Shen Yanling in the common lyrics, so the sentence "A horse arrives at Hongtong" has no basis.

"A horse arrives at Hongtong" means that she was deceived by the procuress and sold to Shen Yanling. It is a false claim that Prince Wang passed the imperial examination and Yutang Chun went to the Tianqi Temple to burn incense to thank the gods, and then went straight to the Shen family in Hongtong County. Judging by reason, Yutang Chun must have traveled by sedan chair and not by horse. If she traveled by horse, she would not have been deceived and taken to Hongtong. The lyric "a horse" may be a mistake, or it is said that "a horse" is a kind of idiom in a certain place, such as the Nanjing colloquialism "go immediately," which means going quickly. It can be asserted that it is definitely not traveling by horse. Nowadays, people like to change lyrics, but they often don't understand the lyrics thoroughly. Why is that?

The most special thing is that when Huisheng sings to "The prisoner should not confess," he suddenly adds five interjectory words, "My lord, sir." Every time I listen to this piece to this sentence, I feel a special taste. People don't know where it comes from. It comes from Bangzi. This play is based on the story of Shanxi Province and was originally a Bangzi troupe script that was adapted by a Pi Huang troupe, and Huisheng was good at Bangzi in his childhood, so he added this. No one else has these five words.

The lyrics of Cheng and Xun's "Yutang Chun" have great discrepancies, which are omitted due to space limitations. If we compare them with Mei Lanfang, Shang Xiaoyun, and the old lyrics, the differences are even more numerous. "Yutang Chun" is a must-learn play for Qingyi actors, and the lyrics must be carefully selected, so I have listed a few points for reference.

Lu Talk 173

— Chen Boying

In the past, Zhang Jiaying saw the autumn wind rising and missed the beauty of the Lu sliced fish and soup. He immediately ordered a carriage to return. The Lu fish has since become a historical reference for lyric writers. Among its flavors, the four-gill Lu fish of Songjiang is considered the best. My friend Mr. Tang is from Songjiang, so I asked him about it. Mr. Tang said that all the Lu fish in the world have two gills, but this one has four. It is produced under the Xiuye Bridge outside Songjiang City. Its head and cheeks are bulging, making it look fierce and hateful. It only appears when it is cold. It is most expensive before the winter solstice when it has no eggs inside, sometimes costing several times as much as ordinary fish. People don't value it much when it has eggs inside. It is best to cook it with chicken soup. Not much of it is produced each year, generally because its species is not easy to breed. It is said that Lu Chunyang passed by Songjiang and ate it and praised it, saying that it is beautiful because it is rare. If the species becomes very abundant after a few years, the taste will definitely deteriorate, so he used a spell to prevent it from increasing or decreasing year after year, which is a ridiculous story. When Su Dongpo traveled to Chibi in the Song Dynasty, the so-called Lu fish of Songjiang with huge mouths and fine scales could not be found in the new autumn. It is another kind of fish that is narrow and long like a knife fish, with only one spine and no other bones. The one with a line of black dots on its back that is six or seven inches long is the best, but it is still inferior to the four-gill one. I recorded it and told those who make food recipes.

Record of the Seventh Anniversary of Qingxin School 174

— Yue Jing

The high-rise buildings of the Shanghai Qingxin Middle School for boys and girls stand opposite each other on Lujiabang Road, in a grand and imposing manner. There are many students, and their academic achievements are highly regarded. Its history is the longest in the country. Since the National Government established its capital in Jinling, Chinese people have been vying to reclaim educational power. The school naturally succeeded, and Master Zhang Shilin was appointed as the principal. Mr. Zhang worked hard to renovate the school affairs, which became even more developed. This autumn marks the seventh anniversary, and a grand celebration was held for three days. The 13th of the month was Student Day, and guests attended the forest dance club. The singing and dancing were ethereal and dreamlike. The 14th was Parents' Day, and the strongman Peng Fei performed in the school playground, with a 2,500-pound car running over his body. Also, Mr. Wang Huaying (a Qingxin student) performed magic tricks, biting coins and swallowing tin, suspending people in the air. The programs were truly amazing and pleasing to the audience. The 15th was Alliance Day, which was the most lively and the last day. Yan Society's box office hired Peking Opera actors. Mr. Rong Boming's "Joining the Army" and Shu Yanzhai's "Beheading the Son at the辕门" were rare among Shanghai amateur actors. The host of Suiyuxuan and Jin Biyu, the famous Kun actor of the Tianchan Stage, acted as Meilongzhen. The two actors had a beautiful appearance. Such supporting roles are more elegant, and the natural dialogue and acting are particularly special, so the applause was thunderous for a time, and many people praised them endlessly. The new play "Yang Guifei" was performed by the teachers and students of the school. Teachers Zhou Yingcai, Zhang Xuexuan, and Ge Chenjun participated in the play, which was very exciting. It is said that Jin Biyu was very active in this Qingxin anniversary celebration. Mr. Zhang had already embroidered the four characters "Yi Zan Hua" (Art in Praise of Creation), which were about ten feet long and three feet wide, lined with five-colored tassel red satin horizontal shawls. The gift was recorded with the inscription "Presented to Ms. Jin Biyu by Zhang Shilin, Principal of Shanghai Qingxin Middle School." The gift will soon be sent to the Tianchan Stage with Song Tiansheng (because his voice of praise can be heard in the sky, it was titled as Suiyuxuan) etc. to reward the lady's hard work.

Travel Notes in Southeast Asia (82) 176

— Linghua

The Venerable Master Wan also said that the monks of Siam and Ceylon are not as good as those of Burma, and the Chinese monks are too inferior and must be eliminated. I asked that although the Burmese monks can uphold the prohibition against sexual misconduct better than us Chinese, they cannot keep the prohibition against killing, which is also very wrong. Master Wan said that Burmese culture and morality are very high, and monks cannot be despised by others, so they maintain their dignity to the point of killing people. But in my opinion, the Burmese are oppressed and react, so they have a strong reaction. According to the Buddhist precepts, killing and sexual misconduct are both inviolable. The difference between them and Chinese monks is that Burmese monks fundamentally uphold the alms system and do not approach money, so there are fewer opportunities to do evil. China's monastic system has its advantages and big compromises, leading to the decline of monks' conduct. Reforming the monastic system to return to the Buddhist alms system is the top priority. Another difference is that monks in Siam and Burma have extreme freedom to become monks or return to secular life. Some become monks for one day, three days, half a year, or several years. If they want to return to secular life, they can do so at any time. After becoming monks, they are still supported by their families and relatives, which does not burden society, and it is considered an honor, so everyone must go through a certain number of days of monastic life, just like we view academic qualifications. The Crown Prince of Siam must also go through several months of monastic life, like a military service system. In times of turmoil, the military service system is an obligation, but in times of peace, is the three-year monastic system also an obligation? However, once one becomes a monk, they respect teachers, uphold precepts, and serve elders just like monks, which can practice moral habits. The Burmese are so noble because of this. From the above, the Burmese monastic system differs from that of China in five ways: 1. Alms for food and does not cook for oneself. 2. The length of time spent as a monk is free, so one does not have to violate precepts. If lustful thoughts arise, one can return to secular life instead of forcing oneself like Chinese monks. 3. Not eating after noon is a violation of the rules. 4. Not vegetarian because one begs for alms and eats whatever people give. 5. One only believes in Shakyamuni Buddha as a teacher and does not believe in others, because the Mahayana is not the Buddha's teaching.

On the 30th, I moved to Mr. Lin Baohua's place at the Nanyang Printing Bureau. Mr. Lin told me about the history of the Shwedagon Pagoda, saying that when the Buddha was alive, two Burmese merchants went to India to visit the Buddha and asked the Buddha to give them a souvenir. The Buddha gave them a tin staff, a bowl, and several strands of hair. The merchants returned and offered them to the king, and the king built a pagoda to enshrine them. So the history of this pagoda is very long, and it was touched by Buddhism earlier than China. The Venerable Master Daojie said that this pagoda was built repeatedly by the kings of the past and was not built by one king. Once, the king ordered all the officials in the country to work, and a military officer who disobeyed the order was killed. In short, the Shwedagon Pagoda is still well-preserved and beautiful today. Although it was slightly damaged in the earthquake the other day, it is now being repaired.

Warmth in My Heart (321) 177

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 15: Four Walls Ejecting Tears of Sorrowful Red Love, A Full House Overwhelmed by Lingering Green Sentiment

He said there is often a kind of woman whose looks and figure - if you say she has a problem, you really can't find anything wrong with her even if you nitpick. If you say she is beautiful, there is really nothing particularly attractive about her. She just has a "plain" quality. Many beauties often have a small flaw that can actually enhance their beauty. For example, those Western beauties who think their faces are too shiny put on many fake moles, putting one here and one there. That was popular in the last century and is still popular now. For example, smallpox scars are the deadly enemy of a beauty, and no matter how beautiful you are, you are done for. But these pockmarks, if you have one or two in the right places on your shoulder, heart, or forehead, they don't seem annoying. There is also a kind of young man with a stutter, and Zuo Shichen said he has a kind of lovable demeanor. There is also a kind of young girl with a lisp, and Zuo Shichen said she has a charming appearance like Shi Xiangyun in "Dream of the Red Chamber." In short, the overall appearance is already beautiful, and there are some small flaws, which are the so-called flaws that don't detract from the jade. Therefore, the way Green Sentiment's tongue frequently licks her cherry lips is actually considered charming. There is also a kind of habit called squinting. She doesn't seem to notice it when she's sitting there, but when she's moving, her eyes are always looking sideways and her head is always tilted to one side. That kind of squinting habit is just like the party politics in the world today, with left-leaning and right-leaning tendencies. Green Sentiment happens to be a left-leaning and right-leaning element. She often tilts her head to look to the side when she moves. Later, Zuo Shichen asked her if she noticed that squinting habit herself. She said she didn't notice it, but according to her, her environment made her develop that habit. It turned out that in her own room and in the rooms she went out to other people's houses, the rooms were full of reflective mirrors. The walls were full of large dressing mirrors, and the tops of the dressing tables and washstands were also mirrors. Even the wardrobes were covered in mirrors, and even the bed was covered in mirrors. She was just looking at her clothes in the mirror to see if they were wrinkled, if her bangs were messy, if her pants were too high or too low, and if her face was oily. Wasn't she looking at the mirror as soon as she turned her head to the side? That's how it became a habit. Some people say that this squinting appearance is not good, but Zuo Shichen said that a young girl who has fallen into prostitution is already bad enough, is there anything worse than that? Ever since Long Ziyun threw a party at the Yuebin Restaurant that day, the next day it was Zuo Shichen, the day after that it was Ling Zhixiang, and the day after that it was Lin Fanzhi. They were happy every day and always called for courtesans. Every time they called for courtesans, they always called for Green Sentiment for Zuo Shichen. Zuo Shichen didn't refuse either. By this time, Bao Meiyun's cold, which was full of flattery, had already gotten better. Long Ziyun still called for Bao Meiyun but let Green Sentiment go to Zuo Shichen. Often Bao Meiyun, A Su, and Green Sentiment came together, just like:

The Zen heart is not like catkins clinging to mud,

Again following the east wind flying up and down.

What will happen later? Listen to the next chapter for the breakdown.

Liverpool: Spot sales were slow last week, and the futures market was volatile. Although the textile industry and the general situation are showing signs of decline, cotton prices are still firm. The amount of transactions between buyers and sellers is very small. Initially, Egyptian cotton saw a slight rebound due to the decision to reduce the acreage of fine-fleece cotton to be planted in the next three years, but it quickly recovered.

The Chinese Cotton Production Problem 187

Since China opened up to trade, the great powers have relied on unequal treaties to implement their economic aggression policies, regarding our country as their only market. The annual trade deficit recorded in the Customs Easy Book is alarming. The greatest loss is none other than this. Advocating domestic goods to seek self-sufficiency is a national cry. However, there are many paths to advocating domestic goods, and they are not the same. Looking at the imports over the years, cotton goods are the largest, ranking first. Clothing is the first of the four necessities of life. Now, relying on foreign goods, how dangerous is this? In recent years, although the domestic cotton textile industry has gradually developed (the competition from foreign-owned yarn mills is not discussed for the time being), the annual import of cotton goods is still at 200 million taels of customs silver, which means that the trade deficit is more than 100 million taels. Therefore, revitalizing the cotton textile industry to seek self-sufficiency in clothing is a matter that must not be ignored when falsely advocating domestic goods. To revitalize the cotton textile industry, it is necessary to start with expanding cotton production and improving quality in order to enrich raw materials. Now, please briefly explain this.

China is a country based on agriculture, and the rise and fall of agricultural products is of great importance to the livelihoods of the people. However, in recent years, there have been natural disasters and man-made calamities, with virtually no year without them. Almost all agricultural products are trending towards failure. Everything needed for clothing and human use, which could formerly be self-sufficient and have a surplus, is now supplied by foreign countries. What will be the impact on the national economy and the people's livelihood? Is it just the end of cotton production? In the past, when China's mechanical textile industry was not developed, cotton was exported to foreign countries, in addition to what was needed for handmade textiles and clothing, as the largest part of native products for export. Since the Sino-Japanese War, yarn mills have gradually increased, and the amount used has increased. Exports have gradually decreased, and a cotton famine has occurred. Foreign cotton took the opportunity to enter. After the European War, the yarn mill industry presented unprecedented development, and the pain of insufficient cotton was increasingly felt. In recent years, the demand for cotton has increased, but the production of local cotton has not seen progress, resulting in a sharp decline in Chinese cotton exports and a sharp increase in foreign cotton imports. The surplus of decades has changed into a huge deficit.

Youth Corner

Impressions of a Northern Trip 203

— Su Ling

(24) — Dalian

After leaving the Taihua Restaurant, I borrowed a friend’s car from Lao Yang, and we arrived at the front of Tokiwa Bridge and the Tokiwa-za Theater.

The Tokiwa-za is a theater with an interesting architectural design. The stage is a series of receding circular arches.

According to Lao Yang, the Nikko-za is also an interestingly built theater, but its stage is square, the opposite of the Tokiwa-za.

The films shown are not new. "The Three Musketeers" starring Douglas Fairbanks was screened in Shanghai a year ago. In the right corner of the stage, there is a Japanese person translating the subtitles. This is the same as in theaters in Hong Kong.

The enchanting scent of greasepaint and powder from the Japanese women in the front and back of the theater is truly nauseating. It's strange why Japanese women like to use such extremely pungent fragrances. This also reflects the Japanese character, which I feel always carries a barbaric air, like their wide-sleeved kimonos and wooden sandals. Regarding kimonos and wooden sandals, I don't understand why Japan, which is used to embracing novelty, hasn't improved them (?). Perhaps this is like preserving those Buddhist statues, temples, and various strange customs, wanting to show that they Japanese can represent the oriental races?

Originally, Lao Yang wanted to take me to see Japanese Bushido dramas and dances, but I didn't want to go because I was afraid that if I went in, I would come out before finishing watching, which would be too uneconomical.

After the film ended, amidst the noisy and annoying sound of wooden sandals, we also walked out of the Tokiwa-za. However, the quiet and interesting streets that unfolded before my eyes were what I loved the most. These are inner streets without vehicular traffic. Above our heads was a cloth awning, and only the sound of wooden sandals echoed. The streetlights also appeared very leisurely, even though there were many pedestrians.

These streets have a different charm than the night markets of Harbin and are even less noisy and chaotic than the nights in Shanghai.

We then walked into the Silver Sparrow Cafe, which is probably like the famous cafes in Tokyo.

A Japanese waitress, probably only sixteen years old, came up very lively and asked us what we would like to eat. I didn't understand Japanese and didn't have the happiness (?) of conversing with her, so naturally, I had to let Lao Yang talk to her.

It's strange. I don't know why the Japanese use English transliterations for the names of things like oranges and apples. The word "Icecream" is also particularly strange in southern China, being half transliterated and half translated, while in the north, it is completely translated, called "bing gao" (ice cake). Perhaps "Ice Cream" is completely transliterated in Japan.

After we finished eating what we had ordered, we walked out of the Silver Sparrow Cafe.

Walking slowly, we gradually moved away from the beautiful night city and entered the dark and chaotic streets—the place where the Chinese gathered. You could easily smell the aroma of opium and hear the sounds of people arguing. I truly felt the barbarity of our civilized nation.

The Law Society Research Group of the Law School This Week 204

— Yi Xin

No need for much introduction—readers of this publication—all know that the Law Society Research Group of the Law School is a research academic group organized by some students outside of class at the school. Their purity of purpose, openness of attitude, and intensity of work need no elaboration. Here is a brief overview of their work this week to inform those who care about the group.

The lecture was held in the fourth classroom. First, Ms. Jin Guangbai, the president of the group, spoke on "Freedom of Association and Individual Freedom." Next, Mr. Zhao Jianxin spoke on "The Principle of People's Livelihood and Labor Problems." Mr. Chen Anshu spoke on "The Art of Public Speaking." Mr. Fan Shoujian spoke on "The Two Major Problems in the Chinese Youth Circle Today." Due to time constraints, the topics pre-arranged by Zhang Mingjun and others could not be presented. In order to change the silent atmosphere of the meeting and the solemn and quiet taste, Ms. Jin gave a more interesting speech entitled "The Nationalist View of Love," drawing from Lin Daiyu and Jia Baoyu to what view of love we should take. Ms. Jin deeply criticized Daiyu's death as self-inflicted, as she had no courage at all... As for Daiyu's beauty, it was purely a sick beauty. Baoyu also had no bravery, he was just a white-faced scholar. In China, the so-called talented men and beautiful women often take them as representatives, and young men and women often take them as models in love. Men identify with Jia Baoyu, and women identify with Lin Daiyu. Some young men even develop lovesickness for Daiyu after reading "Dream of the Red Chamber," and young women develop lovesickness for Baoyu. It can be seen that Daiyu and Baoyu's love has become the golden rule for young people's love in China. We should actively reject and correct this erroneous concept. At the same time, Ms. Jin further elaborated on a nationalist view of love for two hours before announcing the end of the meeting.

The litigation practice was suspended for one week due to the monthly exam, so two sessions were held on alternating days to make up for the deficiency of the previous week. The chairman of the group, Mr. Shen Deji, is not only quite responsible for this, but he also has a considerable research background in law. Therefore, he is extremely interested in and happy to engage in the moot court practice. The drafted cases for the two practices are attached below.

Second Practice Draft Case

Zhang Shan has been without a child for many years with his wife, and in the fifth year of the Republic, he adopted Li Si's daughter from a nearby family as his adopted daughter. Last year, Zhang Shan and his wife died one after another. This year, his adopted son is fifteen years old. Zhang Hu, Zhang Shan's younger brother, obtained the consent of Li's daughter to betroth her to Wei Bing as his wife. The Li couple heard the news and expressed their opposition, arguing that when their daughter was given to Zhang Shan as his adopted daughter, after Zhang Shan died, the relationship with the adopted son was terminated. How could Zhang Hu act without authority? Therefore, they petitioned the court to determine the right to arrange the marriage and the right of guardianship. Zhang Hu argued that since Li Si gave his daughter to his brother to raise, he had long lost the parental relationship, so how could he come out and interfere? How should this case be judged?

Practitioners

Judge—Chen Gongyi

Prosecutor—Han Yongling

Clerk—Shen Jie

Plaintiff—Lu Zhonglin

Defendant—Chu Kaishen

Plaintiff's Lawyers—Shen Deji—Cheng Enlu

Defendant's Lawyers—Han Kejie—Fan Wei

Relevant Person—Zhang Ming

Third Practice Draft Case

Qiao Shouren of Baoshan had two sons and two daughters. The daughters were named Fengxian and Fengzhen. Fengxian married into the Wu family in Wuxing. Fengzhen married a British man named Brewster, who had become a Chinese citizen, and had been doing business in London for a long time without returning. Shouren was old and ill and died in the first month of the seventeenth year of the Republic, leaving behind more than 600,000 yuan in property, which was equally enjoyed by the two sons. Fengxian received not a penny, which was inevitably disappointing. In the eighteenth year, the detailed rules for the implementation of property inheritance for married daughters were promulgated. Fengxian hired a lawyer and sued the court to re-analyze the result. She won the case and was awarded 200,000 yuan in property. This autumn, Fengzhen returned to the country due to business and saw that her father had passed away. Therefore, she exercised her right to request a re-division based on the detailed rules as a married daughter. How should this case be judged?

Practitioners

Judge—Zhou Wenzhu

Prosecutor—Zhang Xibao

Clerk—T Tiyu

Plaintiff—Jin Guangmei

Defendants—Sheng Shuzhen—Wang Jijin—Wu Wangqi

Plaintiff's Lawyers—Gu Shunliang—Xiao Zhi'ao

Defendant's Lawyers—Fan Zheng—Wang Shilin

Witnesses—Zhu Guangzu—Jiang Xingji

Regarding the latter draft case, Judge Zhou Wenzhu has the most senior trial qualifications, with a very calm and dignified attitude. The questions were also extremely appropriate, pressing step by step and guiding layer by layer, especially when conversing with the plaintiff Ms. Jin Guangmei. The audience listened intently, and after the court adjourned, they praised her incessantly. It is heard that in the next session, Zhou and Jin will be in opposing positions, one as the plaintiff's lawyer and one as the defendant's lawyer. When the eloquent debate begins, there will surely be a grand spectacle.
